O vos, tres chiers filz, je vos ai acomplit cest livre qui est li derriens de la science de medicine ensamble l’emplissement de lui, et ai fait la fin per ses expositions et par ses declarations.	 Oh you, dear readers, I have completed this book which is the foundation of medical knowledge assembled in its entirety and has reached its conclusion through my discussions and explanations.
Et m’est venu en vision que je le vos acomplisse avec cest traitier, qui est partie de l’uevre de mains, c’est a savoir «cyrurgie».	 And it came to me in a vision that I would complete this treatise on surgery, which is part of the work of hands.
Et por ceu que l’uevre de mains est fortraite en nostre region et est etraingie dou tout en tout, si est perie li science et decopee, et n’est riens demorez de li fuers que les petites descriptions en livres des anciens que les mains ont muees.	 And because the work of hands is so great in our region and has been extolled throughout all ages, it seems no one can surpass its details as seen in the old books on anatomy which describe how the hands are made.
Et de ceu est venue li error et li vanitez, et sont closes les ententions et est aloignie li science.	 And of this there came an error and the vanity, and close the intentions and align the science.
Or me semble que je la vuel vivifier ensamble l’ordination de cest traitier selonc la voie d’exposition et de declaration et de l’abreviation;	 "It seems to me that I am interpreting this correctly, as it should be explained in detail according to the way of exposition and explanation.
et venrai ensamble les formes des ferremens de cautere, et des autres estrumens de l’uevre avec l’ajostement de la declaration et de preparation de li, sicom il est mestier.	 "The forms of the fire treatment and other aspects related to curing will be explained, accompanied with an explanation of how it is performed.
Et por la raison de ceu que nuls boins maistres de mains n’est trovez en nostre tens, est li ars de medicine eslongié.	 "And because there are no great masters of hands to be found among us, it is the art of medicine that extends.
Et covient celui qui s’en entremet sormonter en la science d’anathomie, si com Galiens dit, tant qu’il saiche la juement des menbres, et les formes et les conjunctions et les separations d’aus, et aient connissance des osses et des nerf et des brais et le nombre d’ous, et le demenement et des voines movans et des reposans, et dou leu de lor issue.	 "It is advisable for someone who becomes enamored with the science of anatomy as Galen did to stretch their knowledge of bones, nerves, veins and arteries, number of them, and the motion and rest of them.
Et por ceu dist Ypocras que li nons avec le non est mout, et avec l’uevre est poc;	 "And for what else does Ypocras not work as expected and the wound care?
et meismement en l’art de main.	 "In addition to this art of healing.
Nos vos disons en l’introite de cest livre que qui n’est conissans des choses devant dites, si se gart qu’il ne chiece en error et qu’il n’ocie les homes;	 "We tell in the introduction to this book that there are certain things that must be done without fail and with precision.
ensi que j’ai veut maintes fois plusors de ces qui s’entremettent de ceste science et si s’abandonent sen science et sens experiment.	 "And so I want to say many times more than those who are engaged in this science, and if they abandon the art of healing.
Car je vis un fol mire qui copa I apostume de scrophules ou col d’une femme, et copa les arteres dou col;	 "I see a fool who does not know how to approach a woman or how to perform an operation;
por coi tant de sanc issit hors que li femme cheit morte entre ses mains.	 Because so many wounds were outside of where they should be, causing death between his hands.
Et vis I autre mire qui traït une piere d’un home d’eaige, et li piere estoit grans;	 And after that, treat a vein in the leg and make an incision into it, cutting through to where it is large
si emporta avec li une piece de la vessie, et fut mors li hons dedens III jors.	 After he removes with him some part of the vein, three people died.
Et je i avoie ja esteit apelez por lou traire, et vis la disposition dou malaide et la grandor de la piere, et soi bien s’on lou tailloit il en morroit.	 "And I saw one who was called the deceiver, and see the size of his veins and their great size; and if he touched them at all, they would soon die.
Et vis I autre mire qui prist en cure I duc de nostre terre qui avoit la jambe brisie, et avec la briseure ot plaie;	 And another doctor who practiced our treatment that had a broken leg and with an abscess,
et li mires plains d’ignorance estraint la brisure sus la plaie as esteles par fort lieure, et ne lassa a la plaie point de xalain, et le lassa ensi I termine;	 and the doctors who lacked knowledge restrained breaking of the bone with too much force, leaving no healing at all to the wound, and left it untreated until the end.
et li comanda qu’il ne la desliast mie;	 and commanded that he not remove the dressing from him;
et demora ensi que li jambe fut toute enflee et li piez et vint a perdition.	 And they delayed until his leg was all healed, leaving it weak, leading to destruction.
Je fuis apelez por venir a lui, et me hastai por venir deslier la jambe;	 I called upon him to come and cut off the leg;
et quant je l’oi desloie si fut em pais et ne sentit point de dolor.	 "And when I dislocated it, it did not feel any pain.
Mais toute voie li corruptions estoit ja confermee ou membre, et ne la poi saner;	 But every way in which the joint is damaged or misaligned will make it unable to heal.
et ne cessa li corrution d’aler par le membre tant que li membres fut dou tout perdus.	 It could not be corrected while the limb was lost entirely.
Et vis I autre mire qui effondra I apostume enchancreit, et puis enflama per le malice de sa signorie.	 And when I saw another way to treat it that worked, and then inflamed through the veins of its cause.
Car chancre, quant il est purs d’umor melancolique, ne covient mie qu’on i(l) touche de fer s’il n’est en teil leu c’on puisse toute oster ce que est corrumpus.	 Because the chancre (a type of ulcerated boil) when it is full of melancholic humour cannot be treated unless you touch it with iron if one can't get to what has been corrupted.
Et por ceu, treschier filz, vos est besoig que vos sachiez que oevre de mains est devisee en II divisions:	 And therefore, when teaching hands, you should know that every hand has two parts:
c’est asavoir, huevre ou il a peril en plusors dispositions;	 it means knowing which side of the body is affected by more serious conditions.
et je mostrerai en chescun leu de cest livre ou il a paour et peril.	 And I will show you in this chapter where there are doubts and fear.
Por coi il est besoig que vos vos en gardez, si que li fol mire ne puissent mal parler de vos.	 You must remember to hold back your feelings so that they do not harm the patient's voice.
Si prenez vos armes en cusenson, et entreprenez vos malaides legierement et fermement, et usez de la millor voie si que per la graice de Deu vos venez a salut et soiez loez;	 If you take your arms in holding them gently and firmly, using the best way that by God's grace you come to health and be healed.
et lassiez les maladies espoantables de grief saniteit;	 "Allow the open sores to heal naturally.
et ostez vos armes de ceu que vos fait douter, et aiez foit en vos si que vos puissiez venir de cestui monde a l’autre de gloire.	 "Do not doubt or fear this; let it happen and you will enter into another world of glory.
Galiens dist en aucuns de ses amonestemens:	 "He has no friends among his family members:
«Ne prenez mie en cure male maladie, que vos ne soiez apelez fol mire.	 "Do not take any illness as an opportunity to insult me.
» J’ai deviseit cest traitier selonc III chapitres.	 "I have translated the text based on Chapter 3.
Li premiers chapitres est des cauteres de feu et dé cauteres de medicine ague, et est li chapitres ordenez de lou chief jusques as piez;	 The first chapters are of fire cauteries and those of medical remedies, and the chapters end with a poem about justice.
et des formes des estrumens, et des ferremens de cautere, et de tout ceu qui est necessaire en l’ueuvre.	 And descriptions of organs, and the instruments used in cauterization, and all that is necessary for doing work.
Li secons chapitres si est de taillier et de percier, et des ventouses et des plaies, et des estractions des saiettes, et des semblans choses;	 The second chapters are of healing and cutting, and wounds, extractions from arrows, and similar things.
et est li chapitres ordenez et les formes des estrumens.	 And the chapters end with descriptions of organs.
Li tiers chapitres est de restorer les dislocations et des torcions, et des semblans choses;	 The third chapter is about restoring dislocations and sprains, as well.
et est ordeneiz des lou chief jusc’as piez, et des formes des estrumens.	 It orders the healing of joints that are painful to touch, and the straightening of limbs.
Ainsois que nos nos remembriens de l’uevre, il covient que je die la qualiteit de l’aide et dou nuisement de chescune complexion.	 In order for our minds to remember the usage, it is important that you give them the quality of help and the degree of assistance they need according to their condition.
Je dis que li qualiteis de l’aide, et dou nuisement, est li plus longe parole et subtilz science et li secrez reponus;	 I say that what is medicine, which includes both diagnosis and treatment, involves more long words and subtle sciences and secret remedies.
et de ceu parlerent li plusors des saiges, et s’acorderent a ceu;	 And because of this people speak longer about wounds and agree on what to do for them;
et me soffisent poc lor paroles, car je redous la longesce.	 I often get tired listening to their long discussions, as it is my longest words that they use.
Je dis que cautere aide universement a toute complexion ou il a matiere, fuer que II complexions:	 I say that cautery can generally help any flesh where there is matter, whether it's the skin,
c’est a savoir complexion chaude sens matere, et complexion seche sens matere.	 or heated skin versus dry skin, and warm blood versus cold blood.
En complexion chaude et seche ensamble matiere, deviserent aucun et dirent que cautere i est grans aide;	 In hot and dry skin, there is no doubt, they said that cautery is a great aid;
et li autre dirent le contraire:	 "They said otherwise:
que cautere ne vaut a maladie que vient de chalor et de sechour.	 "Cautery is not worth more than heat and sweat.
Car li nature dou feu si est chaude, et ne doit mie estre cureiz de chaude maladie par chalor, ne per sechour;	 "Because the fire itself is hot, and it should only be cured of a hot disease by heat, not by cold.
et dist cil qui dist lou contraire que cautere fait grant aide a maladie chaude et seche que vient en cors des homes.	 "And those who dispute this say that cautery provides great help to the cure of a fever and dry illness that comes from the cold outside.
Car quant tu comperes le cors de l’ome et sa moistor a la complexion dou feu, tu trueves le cors froit.	 When you purchase the clothing of someone and their moisture at a place of fire, you cool down the body part with cold water
Et je m’acorde a ceste parole.	 I agree to this statement.
Car je l’ai troveit aucune fois per experiment.	 Because it was tried and found no fault once through experimentation.
Et toute voie, ne s’en entremette mie fuers que cil qui l’a esproveit, et qui conoit par lonc usaige le chapistre des cauteres, et la diversiteit des complexions des homes, et les dispositions et les causes de lor maladies, et les sorvenues et l’espaice dou tens;	 "And in every way they say that those who have experienced it and know how to use the cautery will find relief for their ailments, and remedies, and causes of illness, and all kinds of treatments.
des autres complexions n’avons nos mie paour, meismement em maladies froides et moistes.	 "And for other types we have our own doubts as well, whether it be cold or wet diseases.
Et tuit li mire s’asemblerent et s’acorderent au cautere.	 And they assembled and agreed with the cauterization.
Et sachiez, filz, que cautere ensamble feu si est des secrez des cures, et de plus grant bonteit que cautere de medicine ardant.	 "And remember," friends, that fire cure is gentle yet strong; it should be applied to wounds with great care.
Car li feus est simples, et ne vient mie fuers que au membre qui est cuis, et ne nuit a autre membre se poc nom.	 "Its effects are simple: only the member being burned will feel pain, and no other part of the body will be affected.
Les medicines ardans vienent de membre a autre en aloignant, et font venir au membre maladies de grief sanation;	 "Burning remedies come from one part to another, and bring about the healing of pain in illness.
et par aventure ocit lou malaide.	 And through time
Li feus por sa hautece et por la bonteit de sa substance ne fait mie ceu, s’il n’i a superfluiteit.	 Nor does the heat and good health of its body prevent it alone if there is not enough
Et ceu vos ai je troveit par experiment et par la longesce dou servise et de l’estude que j’ai mis en l’art, et esteit sus la verteit des choses;	 And through experimentation and the length of my service and study that I have put into it, there was a breakthrough in the art,
et por ceu je m’escuse de la longesce de la parole, car il ne me plait mie que je vos oste le secreit qui est reponus ou feu, et la qualiteit de l’uevre, coment il deboute les maladies des cors, si com li philosophe le dit en demostrant;	 and for the sake of sparing words because it does not please me to reveal what is hidden or fire, and the quality of the blood, as long as he is treating diseases with his own hands, as a philosopher says when demonstrating.
or le recevez en vos pensees.	 And I forgive you in my thoughts.
Et sachiez, fil, que il s’acorderent en quel tens doient estre faites les cauteres, et eslirent prientens.	 "And have it understood, dear one, that you must apply the cauterizing procedure.
Et je dis que cautere est covenable en tous tens, por ceu que li nuisemens sorvenans est desoz mis par l’aide dou cautere;	 And I say that cautery is beneficial to all people because the healing of wounds comes through the help of cauterization.
et meismement se li cauteres est por dolors necessaires fors et hastans que ne puent atendre le tens que plus grans malice ne veigne au membre.	 Also, cautery is most beneficial for necessary pains and haste to prevent greater evils from occurring in the member.
Et n’i pensez onques, chier fil, si com font li fol mire;	 And do not think any more, dear friend, as long as they stay still.
car a la maladie qui est sanee par cautere n’a point de revenue;	 because the disease cured by fire does not have an end to it
et il le dient ensi;	 and he will die eventually;
mais il n’est mie si com il cuident, por ce que cauteres nen est que medicine qui mue la complexion, et seche les humors que sont cause de la dolor, et vaut mues que medicine por le hastement de sa valor, et por la vertut de son oevre et de sa signorie.	 However, caution must be taken when using fire therapy as it is not a cure-all for the complexion and dries out humors that are related to pain, and may cause wounds in doing so quickly.
Et possans chose est que li maladie viegne aucune fois selonc la complexion dou malaide et lou leu de la maladie et sa vertut;	 And one can be sure that the disease will not return again according to the complexion of the patient and his body's health.
et sont assemblees en lui les superfluitez par l’aquisition des viandes et des semblans choses, se ce n’est cauteres administrez em leu ou il ait poc de superfluitez et de moistor, si com cauteres de dens por la dolor, et les semblans choses, et teil dolor ne revient mie;	 and they will be eliminated by the acquisition of meat and similar things if caution is not taken when using fire therapy, as burns may occur due to dryness or moisture, so it's important to avoid excessive dryness and excess moisture.
mais ce avient poc.	 But this happens quickly.
Et mout de gens n’entendent mie por coi cauteres est apelez li derriens de medecine, et c’est voir;	 And many people do not understand when they hear the word "cautery," and it's clear to see
mais il ne croient mie que cauteres vaille aprés medicine, mais lor ententions est fause, et est cauteres li derriens de medicine por ceu que quant nos aministrons manieres de cures en aucune maladie et elles ne valent, adonc administrons nos le cautere, et il vaut.	 They do not believe that cauteries are only after medicine, but their intentions are false, and cauteries people for the reason that when we administer our manner of cure in any disease they don't hold value, after we administer our cautery, it is valuable.
Adonques apert bien que cauteres est li derriens de medicine, ne mie selonc l’entention des folz mires.	 "And if you truly understand the importance of cauterization after medicine, do not follow the intentions of those who are mistaken.
Li ancien dirent que cauteres d’estrument d’or est muedres que de fer, et ne dirent ceu fuers que por la qualiteit de l’or et por la hautece de sa substance;	 The former said that cauteries of gold are more effective than those made with iron, and they did not say what else was different about gold or iron.
et dirent que li leus de cautere ne fait mie porriture, mais ceu n’est mie voir car je l’ai esprovei, et ai troveit que c’est voir en aucuns homes;	 And they said that the needles used in cautery do not harm the patient but it is difficult to see because I have tried and found that it is seen by anyone.
et cauteres d’or vaut mues que de fer, si com il lou dirent.	 And cauteries of gold are more valuable than those made with iron as they said.
Et toutevoie quant tu chaufes estrument d’or, tu ne seis mie quant il est chaus par la color de l’or, et s’est tantost refroidiez;	 And whenever you heat it with fire, you will not know how much it is burned by the heat of gold, and if it is burned so much that it cools off.
et s’on le chaufe trop;	 If it is heated too much
si font au feu;	 if you burn it with fire
et ensi i a assez d’empechement.	 And the heat will cause it to stop overheating
Et por ce usons nos de cautere de feir que nos l’avons mues apparilliet a nostre oevre.	 And through our means of applying fire cure, we have shown its utility to our work
Or vos ai ordeneit cest chapitre des lou chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que li voie soit plus legiere a trover.	 This chapter teaches the patient how to perform gentle procedures that make it easier for them to find relief
dou cautere olivaire	 Olive oil cautery
Cist cauteres vaut a moistor et a froidor sus lou cerveil, et en i a dous c’on fait par la cause d’une maladie qui est apelee «soda», et par la cause de maintes humors qui dessendent dou chief as eulz, et as oreilles, et por multitude de songes et dolor de dens et dolor de gorge, et meismement a toutes maladies qui vienent de froidor si com paralisie et sode et apoplexie et semblans maladies.	 Olive oil cautery is painful and can be caused by diseases such as "soda" or excessive humors leading to swelling of the eyes, ears, and many other ailments like migraines, sore throats, and similar ailments that come from cold temperatures causing paralysis, stroke, and similar conditions.
Li forme de cest cautere si est que li malaides soit espurgiez par medicine solutive mondifiant le chief III nuis ou IIII, selonc ceu que li vertus et li eaige et li acostumance dou malaide le puet soffrir;	 The form of this cautery is that the patient's hairs are burned with a solution which relieves the pain and itching for three or four days according to how much virtue and ease and comfort their ailment allows them to endure.
et puis fai rere lou chief dou malaide.	 And then, repeat the process on the affected area.
Et puis le fai seoir croisiet entre tes mains, et mettre ses mains sor som peis;	 Then hold it between your hands and put its hand next to you
aprés met la racine de ta palme sus la racine de son neis entre ses II eulz;	 After that, place the root of your palm over the base of his eye between their two eyelids;
et lai ou venra tes dois moiens, si saigne d’enche puis eschaufe le cautere qui est apelé «olivare», de coi ci est li forme:	 and when you remove it from its place, if there is blood, then apply the fire cure called "olive oil," which has this shape:
Et le met sor le leu signiet d’encre, et fai en dessendant et en estraignant ta main poc et poc en trestornant;	 And hold tightly your left hand gently and gently remove it.
puis lieve ta main isnelement, et rewarde le leu se tu vois l’os I sol petit;	 Then let go of your left hand slightly, and release the joint you see in front of your little finger
et se tu ne lou vois, si rencomence le cautere tant que tu voies l’os si com je lou t’ai dit;	 And if you don't see it, as long as the cautery is applied and you can feel the bone like I described earlier;
aprés pren I poc de seil, et met en awe et molle coton dedens, et met sor le leu, et li laisse III jors;	 After taking a small piece of cotton gauze, apply it gently and softly on top of the wound, place it over the area to be cauterized, and leave it in that position for three days;
aprés met sus cotun moilliet en burre;	 After you have burned through the cloth,
et laisse sus tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	 burn until the skin is healed.
aprés cure la plaie de l’oignement qui est apelez «tetrafarmaçon», tant qu’il soit sanez.	 After curing the wound that has been called "Four-arm," as long as it heals completely.
Et se dirent li ancien, que quant plus demoure overte li plaie, plus s’espurge;	 And they realized that when you apply more heat to a wound, it becomes more swollen;
et por ce si aide mues.	 And for this reason I am helping you.
Et dirent aucun de ces que on doit tant lassier le cautere que partie de l’os soit arse, et puis rese on ceu qui est ars de l’os, et soit curez.	 And they say that one must be very careful with the cautery as part of the bone may become burned and then treated as such.
Et dient li autre c’on doit le cautere tant lassier sus, et bouter si fort c’on abaite de l’os ausi large comme I vertoil que les femmes mettent en lor fusez por ceu que les humors issent mues hors;	 And it should be done gently and firmly to prevent the bone from breaking off as much as possible, just like how women put on their jewelry for fear that they will break a bone.
et doit on lassier la plaie longement overte;	 The wound should be held open longer than necessary
aprés le doit on curer et sodeir.	 After the cure, it must be treated and dressed.
Et ces II manieres de cauteres ne me semblent mie estre bones dou tout en tout, fuers qu’en aucuns homes ou il ait voie de paor;	 And these two methods of cauterization seem to me to be no better than any other way, unless there is a fear involved.
et mues me semble que je lou doie laissier;	 I think that leaving it up to you seems like the best idea.
car li chiés li est afoiblis par les solutions continuees de nature, si com nos le tesmoignons ens autres membres;	 because dislocations occur due to continuous natural solutions, just as we have seen in our other members;
et meisme quant li chiés dou malaide est foibles par nature, et li premiere semblance de cautere est plus salve et muedre por moi, et de celi use je oevre en donques emsamble salut.	 and I think that when dislocations are caused by a weak muscle, the first attempt at treatment is more gentle and mild, to which end it is used in such cases.
de l’anciainne dolor dou chief	 "The main pain arises from
Quant en tout le chief vient dolor croniques, et dure longement, si doit user li malaides yeris et pilules qui sont apelees «cochie», et d’espurgement de chief et d’oiles et d’emplastres;	 When all the chronic pain comes and lasts a long time, you should use ointments that are called "poppies" and purgatives to purge excess phlegm and oils from the body.
et s’on li fait le cautere que nos avons devant dit, et il ne vaut.	 And when they perform the fire cautery as we have described, it is not effective.
Pren warde se li chiés dou malade est de fort nature, et qu’il ne soit trop froit;	 If a dislocation occurs due to a strong force and it cannot be easily corrected
adonques le cauterize desoz celui cautere un poc que nos avons dit desus.	 Unless the fire cautery is performed as we have described, you should not perform it in that way.
Aprés fai cautere sus chescune corne dou chief jusc’a l’os, si com devant avons dit, et fai I cautere ou leu qui est apelez «vasselz»;	 After performing the fire cautery on joints of the head near the bone, as we have described, and perform the cautery using a small tool called "scalpel.
et est I leus en coi on met ventouses;	 And you put into them a small amount of water.
et alige ta main si que tu ne voises mie jusc’a l’os:	 And hold your hand so that it does not move near the bone.
li malaides sent trop plus grant dolor en cest cautere que as autres, et je em parlerai aillors;	 In this procedure, pain is significantly greater than in other procedures.
et covient que li cauteres des cornes soient plus subtis que cil dont on cautere la moieneteit dou chief, et c’est li forme:	 The fire cupping should be done more gently using smaller cups that are not used for the main vein of the head.
dou cautere dou chief	 The first sentence of the medieval medical treatise translates to:
Quant en une partie dou chief vient dolor sodaine, et est estendue li maladie jusc’a l’oil, et li chiés est espurgiez par medicines mondifians, et on a fait les autres cures que j’ai dit en la division des maladies, et tout ceu ne profite mie:	 When one of the joints becomes very painful and is accompanied by an illness that comes from the head, it is often treated with various remedies as in other diseases I mentioned earlier.
adonques li fai cauteres selonc II manieres, c’est a savoir de medicine ague et de feir.	 Once you know how to perform cupping, then you must understand and apply the medicines accordingly.
Li cauteres de medicine ague si est que tu preignes une doce d’alz, et oste l’escorce et le recope I poc as II chiés, et puis fent la temple ou li dolor tient en teil maniere que tu puisses reponre la doce d’alz desoz le cuir;	 The cupping for medicine should be done if you have a hook to remove the arrow from the eye and then fasten it in such a way that you can pull out the arrow shaft without difficulty.
et quant elle sera reponuee si le lie et l’estraint bien et le laisse ensi XII houres;	 Once pulled, if both hands are held tightly and restrained well for twelve hours;
et puis le deslie et trait fuers la doce d’ail, et laisse la plaie ensi II jors ou III;	 "And then apply a dressing to cover it up, leaving it exposed for two or three days.
puis met sus cotun plongiet en burre tant que porreture en isse.	 "Then place the cold compress on the affected area until relief is felt.
Aprés le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	 After curing a burn when it has healed completely;
et se tu vues si fai ceu d’aucunes medicines comburans que j’ai escrites ou dozime traitier des medicines comburans.	 "And if you have any more burns to treat, I will provide further instructions on how to apply the healing medicines.
Li cautere de fer si est selonc ceste meniere.	 Fire cautery, proceed as follows
Chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	 Prepare the fire cautery as described below.
Et est apelez «clos» por ceu que li chief est fait a la forme d’un clo ou il ait I poc de corbeure, et em mileu a une petite apparance;	 "And it is called 'closure' when the wound has taken on the shape of a scar or if there are only small scars.

tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	 While it is calm, while he drinks water
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;	 Restrain the joints from moving.
et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier;	 And hold their arms steady so they do not move further.
et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;	 and cover his body with a cloth to prevent the cautery from touching any other part of his body except for the area being treated.
puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;	 Then apply the cautery to his entire arm while holding onto his hand and wrist until you reach the bone, if there is no bleeding on the first application of the cautery then reapply it gently.
et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;	 And wait patiently as the joint does not move when performing the cautery.
que tu ne le brulasses;	 Don't burn him further.
et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	 And that he will live without any other harm occurring.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	 "And when you come close to a fire, your wounds are of no value.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;	 And apply the cautery gently according to their size and large people larger according to their size.
aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	 After applying the third procedure, let them shave their beard as long as they are even.
aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;	 After the other procedures have been performed and it is well healed, let them shave their back as long as they are even.
et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	 And consider making his nostrils long and straight so that he does not snore in bed.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors;	 After the third procedure, when they want to get up, give them a well-made bandage and apply another one.
et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;	 And let him rest well, work slowly, be wary of excessive drinking and eating, and have too high a fever.
et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	 When the lesson is completely healed.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	 After curing the fire cautery, I will tell you later about other treatments for this patient.
de la routure dou ventre	 The womb's lining
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur;	 When the others wounds heal over and are closed up, you should see that they do not grow any more, at which point you apply another cautery as per its quantity, and then close it with glue.
aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit;	 After applying the treatment as we have described;
et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	 and none of the elders had advised to cauterize at three points in this manner
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	 And first make an incision into the joint and then draw it out wide with a line to hold the dislocation in place, making sure not to cut through the bone of the arm.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	 The first cauterization is lighter and easier.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	 There was no pain in any member
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	 When there is no pain in any member, whether of a blow or an injury, and the pain lasts on until it subsides; but when it comes to cauterizing at the point where they are called 'pricks', and also cauterize them according to their length and smallness, and their flexibility, location of torcs and suffering.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien;	 If the patient is well after the first cautery it should be fine;
se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	 if the patient's condition does not improve after the first one, then proceed to another cautery as custom is that it should be done on the nearest limb where the pain persists;
de meselerie	 Melioration
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	 There is no cure for the disease once it has been caused by cauterization and primarily comes from the decomposition of blood and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief:	 You cannot cauterize the veins; if his illness is at its onset, and he has been cured according to what we have said in this division, and you doubt that there will be no more pain or suffering, until you perform the cautery on the head
I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous;	 I cut off his nose to one end, and towards the front at its finish.
et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel;	 "And he will have trouble with his toes.
et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir;	 "And he will hold the eye steady as long as possible until the blood from the veins has stopped.
et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	 "He will cautorize his nose according to what is in front of him.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse;	 "And the dizziness occurs everywhere.
et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules;	 "And it becomes clearly visible if you hold the cautories that we have mentioned or chief, and one cauterizes on the nose, another on the eyebrows, a third above the eyes, four below the eyes, five above the cheeks, six below the cheeks.
et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains;	 "And two on the cheeks, and two on the forehead above the eyebrows, one at each hand joint, and below the elbows.
et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler;	 And if you wish to cut them off at their roots while they are growing, do not burn them.
et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	 Do not use a fire cautery on the arm's bone or any other bone in the body except for the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite;	 And as you do more cauterizing, you will find more help and benefit from it.
et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	 It is because the nerves are already damaged that there is no pain when cauterizing if done correctly as the skin becomes charred and crisp.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	 "It is important to make sure the patient's hair grows long and even, as that will help guide them through various procedures.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	 After curing the left arm with honey and other treatments until it is well healed.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre;	 When a member becomes inflamed and is treated with ointments and plasters, and it does not improve after attempts at cauterization of the limb depending on its size and smallness.
et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur;	 And if you make a fire through the vein's hole.
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then treat the wounds until they heal.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure;	 "And once the cautery is applied to the hand and foot, it prevents movement of the member, except if it moves freely.
et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	 "And whenever there is no constraint on the arms and legs moving as they should, none of this occurs.
de albaras	 of the shoulder
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color;	 "When the disease called 'albaras' is cured by cautery, and the physician knows nothing about it, he applies a little cautery according to how much blood can be drawn in one go, as long as the bleeding continues and stops at the same time.
puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie;	 "Then he applies a powder of flaxseed and lentils with rose petals and leaves from the same plant. And for hemorrhoids, for an abscess in the anus, or any kind of sore;
et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	 "And bind it all together with linen bandages, and put it on his back as long as he is conscious.
li cure de chancre par cautere	 The treatment of chancre (scrofula) through cautery
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	 When a chancre appears at the outset, and you see it arrest, if you cauterize with a fire cure by burning an even circle around it.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre;	 And all of them said to do cautery as for ulcers.
et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois;	 But I think it's not right because I doubt that he will be healed and cured completely, so I do not wish to try this at all.
et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	 The second part of the sentence means that if you perform a fire cautery, which is known as "circulation," just like we said in our previous example.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	 The elbow cannot stay still
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens;	 When someone has an ailment called "abdubing," and it is about to die or from the excess of moisture causing it to swell excessively and he has pain, whether through the tendons.
et tu la vues haster de meurer:	 And you have seen that it will die.
adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant;	 Unless the cautery is performed on ulcers punctually.
aprés le laisse ensi.	 After leaving it alone.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	 She will grow ill from working too hard.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	 And if you give them the complete treatment as prescribed by the doctor or physician

While treating them for 'adubelati' illness as long as the cautery continues and if given a complete course of treatment which is prescribed by the doctor, then it will cause the sores to heal in a manner so that the flow of blood is restored in such a way that the course of disease is eased.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	 After the cure has been perfectly performed
li cure dou feu par fer	 cautery with fire
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	 Another way to treat disease is by "burning," and nothing else than the burning of member
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est;	 If you see this ailment in the left that can cause suffering, avoid using sharp and large forceps. Instead, use small ones as advised by the doctor or surgeon.
aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	 After all cauteries are performed and there is no longer any infection or contamination present in the area, nothing of what was corrupted should remain intact, everything that has been corrupted must be destroyed.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	 And then let it rest for three days and put on the burns with oil so that the burns of fire are healed, and all the corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	 After the treatment of burned members

mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division:	 But all cauteries of fire are worse in every way and I have already explained the treatment for this condition by dividing it into two parts:
pren la quant tu en as mestier.	 Take what you have read earlier.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	 The hairs that come out
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	 It occurs many times when piercing through the skin is a disease called "closes" according to our understanding, and it is a very painful thing that causes harm.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	 The cauteries of this disease are done in two ways.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	 It is to know fire cautery and hot water cautery.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges;	 "The fire cure is that you should shave and make it smooth like a mirror, so when the hair prickles at their base, hold them steady to prevent movement until they grow.
aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou;	 "After applying it all over the finger, keep your hand tight around the prick as long as the prickling continues on both sides of the finger.
et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture;	 "And leave them in place for three days until they stop itching and peeling off.
puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	 "Then apply a salve of bitter water with it to the skin and let it be smeared all over at night; and after dawn remove what is not necessary from its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	 "After curing the dislocation, it must remain fixed as long as its bones are aligned.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude;	 "And if they are converted by blows to the head and many times occur in hands and feet, it is advisable that you apply a hot cure.
et est en teil maniere:	 "And do so like this:
pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues;	 "Take a nail or any other sharp object, and stick it into the vein's hole and artery. This is important because puncturing veins can be dangerous.
et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine;	 "Stick the nail into it until it pierces through entirely, then apply some hot oil and keep your hand steady as you pull back the edge of the nail towards the base of the vein. This is important because puncturing veins can be dangerous.
et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre;	 "After applying hot oil, let it sit for an hour.
puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	 "Then remove the nail and allow it to fall out completely at its root.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	 "Afterwards, while you are working on the rest of the body, also treat any burns that may occur at the joints.
li cure dou trembler	 The patient is instructed to tremble.
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee;	 "If any of the fingers or toes are trembling from coldness, or if they are numb in some way, it is important to perform four burns on each big toe and one burn between the small toes.
et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire;	 And you shall instruct them to have a heartburn cure with olive oil.
si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	 They will make the patient's cold symptoms worse if they tremble or hold tightly onto their illness.
des pustules puans	 pus filled blisters
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	 No such thing is evident on the surface of the body or pustules are present that come from infected substances.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule:	 It is advisable to perform a fire cure as soon as you notice that one of the sores has become inflamed
un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	 A subtle application of a mixture, which can either be applied to the fire so it is held in place or rubbed into the root of the abscess, or onto a long lance for cauterization.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez;	 And once the cure is applied in this manner and it becomes clear that there will be no bleeding to speak of, but rather all superfluous fluids which are present.
mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	 But you should perform this procedure after the evacuation of wounds is complete.
quant li artere est copee	 The shoulder joint has been dislocated
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses;	 There are often large eruptions of blood from the artery which is cut near the wound or at the incision point, and similar things occur in other parts of the body.
et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	 "And there comes great pain from misalignment.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus;	 "And whenever this occurs, whether you apply pressure on the vein's wound or not, hold tightly as long as it does not stop bleeding by itself.
puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge;	 "Then apply fire cupping to the affected areas more intensely and for a longer duration until they turn bright red;
puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	 "Then apply cupping with one or both hands depending on the size of the wound and its location; place it over the vein where you hold your hand, and keep it in place as long as it does not stop bleeding.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	 And when you remove your thumb from the vein and the cautery is released, if a more intense cautery that has been set on fire is applied quickly to it.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez;	 "And do not cease to perform this one after another until they are stopped;
et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide;	 "And make sure you do not harm the nerve that is related, and nothing else occurs on or near the wound.
et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit:	 "And when the artery is severed and cannot be reattached immediately due to its great size, then it can only be treated in one of these ways that we have mentioned:
ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc;	 "or by cautery, or by extraction when it cannot be treated immediately, or through very high pressure applied to the artery, or with medical treatments that can help repair the damage.
et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	 "And should hold still and remain still.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	 "Consult the medical practitioner about any additional treatments that may be prescribed or required.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne;	 "And if it occurs without any medical treatment being available, then place your fingers over the wound as we have mentioned and tightly hold until the wound is closed.
et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez;	 "And do not move it should remain still as the cold seeps through to prevent freezing and frostbite from occurring.
et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	 "But if he has experience with cauteries or medical treatments, then perform them first.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	 The second book of medical treatments
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres;	 Here is the translation of the opening sentence: "We have spoken about the first chapter in which it is advisable to use fire cautery or other medicinal treatments and remedies for wounds.
et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	 And in the following chapter, we will discuss this matter more thoroughly because it is a crucial part of our work.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	 And so that you know, when it comes to this chapter, there is more risk and fear than in the first chapter, because of this reason one should use them with greater caution.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses;	 In the following chapter, there are often evacuations of blood when opening veins and incisions near vital areas. It also covers treatments for wounds, extractions of arrows, and cutting into stones.
ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	 And in that chapter, there is often doubt and fear, resulting in many deaths.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	 And I assure you to proceed with care.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	 Because people come for treatment.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice;	 if a person is so sick with their illness that they die due to the severity of their disease and the strength of their pain.
et de ces doit on avoir paor.	 And of these must have fear
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit:	 You shall know it is time.
