puis le deslie en cele maison meisme tenebrouse, et esprueve sa veue, et lou fai veoir aucunes choses, et puis li remet lou lien jusc’a septime jor;	 "Then let it be removed gently in a quiet place and remove its head and view everything closely without moving. And then tie the cord tightly once more.
et ne covient mie que tu faices ceu en l’oure de la cure ou aprés l’incision maintenant, mais il covient que tu aliges ceu, por ceu que li aigue monte hastanment.	 "It is only necessary to do this in the course of treatment or after cutting but it is important that you do so for safety.
se apostemes chaus vient, que tu desliies l’oil devant le septime jor, et l’adrece de ceu qui assouaige aposteme;	 When you come to a joint, apply ointment on it while facing the ninth hour, and cleanse with it what touches the abscess.
et quant il est apaisiez, si deslie la veue et met sus sa faice I orilliet por covrir aucun jor, et soit adés en celle maison tenebrouse.	 When you are done applying ointment to all joints and have come to the ninth hour, if there is any bleeding from wounds, you must wrap them with cloth so they do not show in light.
Et puis isse de la maison poc et poc, et se convertisse en ses cas;	 And then turn it into its own case and cases that come to be like that.
et saiches que nulz deciples ne se doit entremettre en cest cas.	 Then you should not enter in this case.
Et uns vint a nos qui estoit de la Yrach, qui nos dist que en som pais faisoit om almagda perciet, a coi on succe l’aigue, mais toutevoie je n’en vis onques nul en nostre terre, ne je ne lou lis onques en livres des anciens;	 And there was one of the Saracens who said that in some places people used magic to make things grow, but we do not see any evidence of it here or anywhere else in our land, nor have I seen any evidence of it in books written by the ancients.
et par aventure c’est une novele chose.	 And by chance this is a new thing.
Et ce sont les semblances des formes de almagda, por ceu que cil qui ne les conoit les voie;	 These are the likenesses of magic things, since those who do not know them see them like that.
et soient d’arain proprement:	 "and let them grow naturally
Et soient li chief d’aus de ceste meisme subtiliteit, et li derriene en III angles ague.	 "These chiefs have great subtlety and they deceive in three ways.
de la char sor le neis	 "from the burn until the wound
Aucune fois naissent ou neis chars ajostees diverses, de coi il i a aucunes qui semblent scorpions a mout de piez;	 There are no hairs that prick the vein or make any other type of injury.
et si i a de telz ou il ait char enchancree de fuxe color, et si a char souef de bone color.	 If they have been burned with heat and pain, if there is severe burns in white hair.
En celle donques de ces chars qui est souef, et ne mie enchancree, covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains encontre lou soleil;	 When the hairs that are burned do not heal and become damaged, it is important to keep them between your hands in direct sunlight.
et oevre ses narines, et giete l’oncine a celles chars, et les trai fuers;	 And wet the nose of the patient with cool water so they can be applied to the burned hairs and the wounds.
pues cope ceu que tu em pues sostenir au spatumile subtil agut d’une part, tant que tu saiches que celle char est toute ostee.	 Then continue applying a small amount of cool water gently from one side until you know that the hair is completely healed.
Et s’il en remaint aucune chose c’on ne puisse coper, si l’ovrez a tout I des estrumens subtil legierement, si qu’il n’i demoure rien;	 If there are no signs of healing, do not try to apply anything further. Gently massage the affected area with cool water if you need to, without causing any additional damage.
et se sans te sormonte, ou aposteme chaus, si lou secort si com il covient;	 "And do not move your head or shoulders if it is otherwise necessary.
et se c’est apostemes malignes, si te haste et lou cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez et soient ostees toutes les chars, puis giete ou neis aisil et aigue ou vin.	 "And do not harm yourself or the patient with too much cautery as long as they are still alive and all their hairs are intact.
Se li neis oevre, et moistors en vient jusc’a palais, saiches qu’il est sanez;	 "If it is necessary to remove them, do so carefully without causing too much harm as long as they are still alive and all their hairs are intact.
et se moistors ne perce si com il covient, saiches qu’il i a char nee en l’os desus, a coi li estrumens ne vient mie por taillier:	 "And if it is necessary to remove them without causing too much harm, then do so carefully into the bone of the joint.
adonques covient il que tu i boutes I fil de lin un poc gros, et soit noez de mains nous, et ait entre chescun nout d’espaice I doit ou moins;	 "Until it is necessary to cut off one or more hairs gently and carefully with your hands only, and avoid touching any other part of the body except for that.
et mette li malaides lou chiés dou fil en son neif a som pooir, et traie en odorant tant qu’il viegne par lou neif dedens la bouche;	 "And let them grow until they are as long and thick as you like in your own hair. Do not touch the lips or face while growing.
et maintes fois font ensi li enfant as escoles, et c’est legiere chose a celui qui le vuet faire;	 And many times there is an attack on him who tries to do it
puis tien le chief qui vient par lou neif a une main, et l’autre chief qui vient par la bouche a l’autre main, et saiche l’un aprés l’autre en soiant as nous qui sont ou fil.	 And each time the child comes by one hand and then the other by mouth to the other hand, and they do it one after the other while holding onto what is there
Fai ceu tant que tu saiches que li nout ont corrompue celle char, puis trai lou filz, essue le sanc, et moille lou fil en oignement egiptien, et le remet derechief au neis si com devant;	 Do it as much as you can until the evil one has corrupted that thing and then treat them with fire, extract the poison, and burn off the hair in Egyptian fashion, and place them directly on the eyes.
fai ceu III jors ou plus, tant que li oignemens corrode tout ceu qui est demorez de char;	 Do it three times or more, as long as evil spirits contaminate everything that is dear to you
et puis met ou neis une caine de plonc aucuns jors tant qu’il soit sanez, et s’il a mestier de medicines sechans, si en use;	 And then put on the eyes one drop every few moments as long as he is sane and if he needs healing water from medicine that way.
et c’est li forme de l’estrument por purgier lou chief, a coi on distille les oiles et les medicines ou neis:	 And this is the method for purifying the spirit by distillation of oils and medicines you get.
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain, semblant a une lampe overte, si com une cainne, et li conduis ausi;	 And it may happen by fire or water, similar to how one can catch fire, causing
et se tu vues, si fai une cainne close, et soit li estrumens plains por espurgier lou chief;	 and when you see smoke, if there is a flame near
et ait I mainche au chief por lou tenir quant on chaufe l’oile ou aucune liquor.	 And hold the eye tightly to prevent it from moving when one holds an oil or any liquid.
de la char sor le neis	 "from the burn until the wound
Maintes fois naist au chief dou neis une maladie qui est apelee «telul», et croist et devient grans adés, tant qu’il est vis chose au regarder;	 Many times occur to the head with a condition that is called 'tolly', and spreads and becomes large as long as it looks at something.
et por ceu covient que tu lou copes au comencement, et l’oste tout fuer, puis met sor leu lou cautere ou la medicine ardant;	 And to prevent this from happening you should apply the burn treatment or other healing agent as soon as possible.
et s’on le tarde a coper tant qu’il soit grans, si pren warde s’il est durs, de fuxe color, de povre sens:	 And if it is not corrected when it becomes large, and if it gets hard to see clearly, fix the injury;
si ne lou touchier mie de fer car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, car quant on le cope aucune fois, si en vient grant malice au malaide;	 If you don't hold tight enough with fire it can result in a severe infection, as if one fails to correct the injury at all times, and great damage occurs to the eye.
et se li apostemes est de soef touchement, non mie de fuxe color, et tu vois c’on le puisse tout coper, si vuide le malaide et lou cope sens paor, et cure le leu de choses sechans et restraignans.	 The first sentence to translate is: "et se li apostemes est de soef touchement.
quant li neis est copez et cosus	 "When one cannot speak and communicate
Saiches que quant solutions de continuation vient en une de ces cartillagines ovraiges, i profite poc, fuer que en aucuns homes.	 If someone presents a solution to the problem in this chapter of treatments, I will benefit from it, for none are useless
Il covient donques cant ceu avient a aucun, si regarde se li plaie est fresche a tout son sanc;	 It's important when the wound is fresh and covers all its surface.
et adonques ajoste les II levres a une costure, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	 And after stitching two or more layers together, heal as much of it as possible.
et se les levres sont ja desevrees d’une part et d’autre, si covient que tu escorches toutes les parties de lor keur tant qu’elles sainent, puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et l’estraint, et poudre sus poudre de sanc de dragon, et encens broiet;	 And when the layers have healed on both sides, if it is desirable that you clean all parts of their surface as much as they can withstand, then stitch together two or more layers and bind them with a bandage, and powder over the bleeding wound with fine powder and incense.
et met sus les poudres une piece d’emplaustre de fort ou d’autre emplaustre soudant, et le laisse tant qu’il chiece par lui, puis le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And sprinkle over the powders a bit of strong or other fragrant powder to help it dry quickly and heal the wound as much as possible.
Li maniere de la costure si est que tu assembles la solution:	 The manner of suturing is to assemble the solution
ou par aguilles, si com nos avons dit en la costure dou ventre;	 or with needles if you have said in the suturing on the belly
ou par fil, si com je le t’ai fait savoir.	 or with sutures, as I told you
des apostemes des levres	 of the limbs
A mains homes avient dedens les levres aposteme dur, semblans a grains de veces, et menor et plus grant;	 A main fist is dense and hard to cut through veins, arteries and bones.
adonques couvient que tu tornes les levres, et fendes sus chescun nout, et le prent as pinceures et le cope en chescune partie;	 unless you turn the flesh, and shave all around it, and pull on all sides gently and evenly.
puis emple lou leu aprés l’incision de vitriole broiet, tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	 Then apply the new flesh after cutting through a vein, until you are sure of its evenness.
et puis lou leive d’aisil, et cure lou leu de choses seches tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And then apply the new skin and treat it well until it is healed.
de la char des gencives	 Of the joints
Maintes fois naist sus les gencives char ajostee, que li ancien apelent «albulus»;	 There are often convulsions at the sight of a bleeding wound, which people call "a bull.
si covient que tu la sostienes as tenailles, et la cope a sa racine, et laisse corre la bowe ou le sanc;	 If you hold it with needles and keep its root firmly, and leave room for the blood to flow freely or the wound.
puis met sor le leu vitriole broiet, ou autres poudres restraignans et desiccatives;	 After spreading salt on the wound, or other powders restraining and dehydrating;
et se celle char revient aprés l’incision, et maintes fois avient, si la cope la seconde fois, et la cauterize:	 And when the second incision is made, it often happens again.
si ne revient mie aprés le cautere;	 If nothing comes out after the cautery.
et ce sont les formes des estrumens por coper.	 These are the forms of wounds to be treated with cautery.
des sordens	 the sores
Aucunes fois sont assemblees au chief des dens, dedens la bouche entre les gencives, escorces qui sont laides et aspres;	 No such occurrences have been recorded at the root of the spine between the ribs and the diaphragm;
et aucune fois sont li dent noir et citrin et vers, tant que li corruption vient a la gencive, et sont li dent puant;	 And no such cases are recorded when the teeth turn black and white as they decay, until their roots become decayed;
si covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains, et ses chiés soit en ton saint, et reis les dens ou les escorces aperent, tant qu’il n’i demore rien;	 If you make sure that the abscess is between your hands and its opening remains open, and you extract the teeth or sores as they appear, until nothing more happens.
et ensi fai de la noiror et de la verdor, et de la jaunice et des autres taiches, tant qu’elles soient mondees;	 And in doing so you remove blackness and whiteness, and greenness and other stains as they fade away.
et s’on oste ceu que i est a la premiere rasion, c’est boin;	 And if you do as I say at first time, it is good.
se ceu non, si rencomence a rere le secont jor et lou tier, tant que tu aies tout reis;	 But if not, try again after the second and third times, as long as you have tried all of them.
et saiches que li dent ont mestier de diverses formes d’estrumens por reire, selonc ceu que li oevre lou demoustre, por ceu que li raseur dont on reit defuer les dens ont autres formes que cil dont on reit entre les dens;	 And the teeth have different forms of injuries depending on what caused them, for example those from a blow to the mouth will be different from those from between two teeth.
et cestes formes et autres soient avec toi appareillies.	 These shapes and others should also appear with you.
Il covient quant tu cures lou dent de sa dolor que tu tardes dou traire tant com tu pues, car ce ne doit om mie faire;	 It is important when treating the tooth pain to take two tablets as prescribed, because it must not be done otherwise
car c’est une substance mout haute jusc’a donc c’on n’ait point d’excusation dou raier.	 Because that substance has such a high concentration therefore there is no excuse for taking more than prescribed.
Adonques quant li malaides est constrains dou traire, si covient que tu soies certains dou dent doillant.	 After the patient has pulled on his tooth
Maintes fois desoit li dolor lou malaide, et cuide qu’elle soit ou dent saint, et fait traire le boin dent;	 Many times the pain from the abscess should be treated, and it should be done whether or not there is a healthy tooth in front of it.
et toutevoie ne se depart mie li dolor per ceu, tant que li malvais estrais, car nos l’avons ja veut faire a ces sainors;	 "And it shall not move while the pain lasts, as long as they are inflamed, for we have already wished to do this healing.
et quant tu es bien certains dou dent doillant, si covient que tu escorches entor lou dent a tout i. spatumile fort por warder la gencive de toutes pars;	 "And when you are certain of the toothache, it is advisable to soak your hand in cold water.
puis le mues a tes dois ou as tenailles subtilz au premier poc et poc, tant qu’il soit bien eslochiés, puis i afferme bien les tenailles;	 "Then gently apply both hands at first, and then firmly press the veins.
et soit li chiés dou malaide en ton saint entre tes genous, et lou tien bien si qu’il ne se mueve.	 "And if you put pressure on a vein between your fingers, it will hold still as long as you do not move.
Aprés estrai lou dent droitement sens brisier, et s’il ne saut fuer, si prent aucun de ces estrumens et le boute dedens de chescune part legierement, et lou remuef si com tu as fait premier.	 After firmly pulling out the tooth, if it still hurts, then put a gentle pressure on its base and remove gently from any side; after which you will move in order to make sure that no harm has been caused anywhere lightly, and repeat what you have done before.
Et se li dens est perciez et mengiez, si covient que tu l’emplisses de drapelz, lai ou li pertus sont;	 "And if the pain is strong and constant, it may be that your veins are being pinched or constricted. Then wrap them in cloth to release them.
et si l’estraint subtilment as tenailles, que il ne brise a l’estraindre;	 "If you gently hold the veins, they will not break when pressed upon.
et covient mout saigement ovrer entor la gencive por deschaucier lou dent.	 "It is advisable to soak your hand in cold water before applying any medication or remedies for toothache.
Et te done bien en warde que tu ne le brises, et en remaigne une partie, et reveigne au malaide par la malice de la racine plus grans dolors de la premiere.	 And make sure you do not break it and leave some part of the skin, and remove the arrow through the malice of its root causing greater pain than before.
Et te warde que tu ne faices mie ensi com font li ignorant sainor, qui par lor haste et par lor hardiesce brisent aucune fois le charreit, et n’i amenistrent mie ceu que nos avons conteit;	 And may you always do as the learned physician does, who by their swiftness and diligence never break a single bone, nor bring about any harm.
mais font venir aucune fois par l’oquison de ceu grant maladie por les racines que i demorent, ou por lou charreit qu’il brisent, si com nos avons sovent veut;	 Nor may they ever come from a great sickness caused by the roots that fester or break bones as we have seen.
et quant li dens est trais, si lavez lou leu de vin ou d’aisil et de seil;	 And when their tendons are torn if you soak the affected area with vinegar and oil.
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, que sovent avient, si emple lou leu de vitriole broiet;	 The sores they bring that fester may be helped by soaking the affected area in vinegar broth.
et se ceu ne vaut, si le cauterize.	 And if not treated, it will worsen.
Les formes des estrumens, a coi om muet les dens premier, soient a longes pointes et a gros mainches, qu’il ne doublent mie quant tu trairas le dent;	 The extremities of the veins are where they must first be held steady so as to last through many points and large openings.
et ce sont les formes:	 These are the forms.
Et soient de gros membres si qu’il ne ploient mie au traire, et soient de fer inde bien fait, et soient dentez por mues tenir.	 If they are amputated at their base and do not grow back, then they must be made of strong wood, so that they may hold firmly in place.
de la racine des dens	 from the roots of the hairs
Quant li racine demoure au traire, si covient que tu mettes sor le leu coton moilliet em burre I jor ou II, tant que li leus soit amolis, pues i boute les tenailles qui sont apelees «algefri», de coi li chiés semblet bec de soigne;	 When the roots are torn and bleeding, it is advisable to apply wet cotton soaked in burning oil or vinegar until they clot.
et soient dedens faites ausi com une lime et c’est li forme:	 And let them grow as a single piece, like this:
Et se les racines ne vuellent issir a tout ces tenailles, si covient que tu descuevre la char tot entor la racine, et i met l’estrument qui est apelez «althali», c’est a savoir palainche, de coi ci est li forme:	 And if the roots will not stay tied to these hairs, it is advisable that you cut off all the hair and expose the roots.
Et soit fors et gros si qu’il ne brise mie, et se li racine saut par ceu, c’est boin;	 Let the hairs be thick and coarse if they do not break off cleanly.
se ceu non, si t’aide de toz les estrumens, de coi les formes vienent ci aprés:	 If this does not happen when using these methods, then it is likely that there was a problem with the method used;
Et si s’aide on de cest estrument qui ait II rains, de coi ci est li forme:	 If there is an instrument with two handles, how do you hold it?
et d’autres ferremens qui sont devant en la rasion des dens, et de cest estrument qui semble unes grans tenailles, dont ci est li forme:	 The other tools that are meant for tightening up the roots and the instrument with large handles whose shape is...
Et soit cist estrumens fors qu’il ne puisse brisier, et saiches que mout d’estrumens de dens sont;	 Or if the hairs are thick and coarse and still break off easily, then it is likely that many of them have already broken.
et ausi d’autres estrumens, qui ne sont mie contez;	 And these other hairs which do not count as yet;
et li saiges maistres subtilz trueve par soi meisme son estrument, selonc ceu que ses ovraiges et li maladie li demoustre, car il i a de teilz maladies ou li ancien n’enseignerent point d’estrument por la diversiteit d’au;s et s’om brise point dou charreit ou des autres os, ou il porrit, si i cerche as estrumens qu’il i covient, que je t’ai dit, et t’aide des gestes, de coi ci est li forme:	 And the greatest subtleties of this instrument he is to master himself by means of it. for such cases and diseases are rare indeed, or if an instrument was not known before its diversity; and in that case one cannot break a bone, nor any other joint, unless they will, seeking as hairs which may be useful, I have advised you, and shown you the way to do this, like:
Et soient gros et bien tenant por tenir l’os, qu’il n’eschaipe, mais le puisse tenir et oster;	 "And let it rest firmly so that the bone does not slip out.
et puis restoure lou leu de medicines convenant a ceu, et s’il ait en l’os porriture, et elle est petite, si la reis a tout cest estrument:	 "Then apply leeches as medicine and if there is pus in the bone, it will be small enough to use with this instrument.
Quant li dent apperent ne mie selonc lou cors natureil, et li forme est laide, et meismement en femmes puceles, si covient que tu saiches se li dens est neis aprés lou dent, et n’est mie en droit leu, et on ne lou puet soier ne limer:	 "When the teeth are set in place naturally and their shape is good, and especially in women who have pulled them out with tweezers instead of pliers, they do not move after the tooth, it is right to pull, but only gently, as otherwise they can damage or break.
adonques lou raie;	 "until the root has been removed;
et s’il est aers avec lou dent, si prent cest estrument dont ci est li forme, et est semblans a I petit bec, et soit de fer inde agut en som:	 "and if you are with tweezers, use the instrument that has this shape and is small enough to fit in your mouth; it must be made of steel and sharp.
Et lou cope poc et poc em mains jors por la duresce dou dent, et por ceu que tu ne mueves les autres, et s’il est apparans c’on le puisse limer, si lou lime d’une teil lime com ci est li forme:	 And gently and steadily hold the tooth in your hand for a while to prevent damage from other teeth, and if you want to remove it, then take that tool whose shape suits best.
et est ausi com li lime de coi on fait les aguilles;	 "It's like using a needle when making arrows;
et en lime lou dent poc et poc em mains jors legierement, si qu’il ne se mueve tant qu’il chiece;	 And when it is very small or barely noticeable, if it does not move as much as you prick.
puis la plaine en la fin a tout aucun raseur, et se li dens est trop trenchans et il blece la lengue, si covient limer l’aspreteit tant qu’il soit igalz, si qu’il ne blece la lengue ne ne corrompe la parole.	 Finally at the end it has no razor and its teeth are too blunt causing damage to the tongue if you try to remove it as much as it is long, otherwise it will damage or distort the speech.
quant li dent lochent	 When the teeth chatter
Quant li dent devant lochent, ou par percussion ou par cheoir, et li malaides ne puet presser sus ceu qu’il menjue qu’il ne chient, et tu les as curez de medicines restrignans, et ceu ne vaut;	 When the tooth is loose or comes out through impact or injury and cannot be pressed back in its place when you try to do so, treat it with restraining medicines.
si les covient restraindre d’un fil d’or, car li filz d’argent devient vert et porrit, mais li ors ne se mue onques;	 If you use a thread of gold as restraint because the thread of silver becomes green and rusted, but the iron is still unaffected.
et soit li filz moiens ne trop gros ne trop menus, selonc la quantiteit de l’espaice entre les dens;	 And if the threads are too thick or thin depending on the space between the teeth;
et se tu vues adrecier les dens, si pren lou fil et lou boute double entre les II dens sains, puis met les chiés entre les dens meus, s’il en i a I ou plusors, tant que tu veignes saigement jusc’au dent sain d’autre part;	 And if you want to adjust the teeth, if you take one thread between two healthy teeth and put them in place. If there is more than one or less, as long as it fits well at the other tooth.
puis rencomence la coverture jusc’a la partie ou tu encomensas, et estrains ta main subtilment et saigement, tant qu’il ne se mueve point;	 "Then cover it gently with your hand, holding it gently and steadily until you have no more movement.
et soit ta lieeure a la racine dou dent si qu’il ne puist eschaper.	 Or if they prick at their base of the tooth.
Puis cope les chiés dou fil a unes tenailles, et les assemble, et les repont entre le dent sain, et le met ensi qu’il ne blece la lengue;	 Then bind them securely with threads, and tie them together, so they are between the sound tooth and the mouth.
et puis le laisse ensi estroit tant com il puet demorer, et s’il deslie, ou li filz ront, si l’estraint d’un autre fil;	 Then let it stand as still as possible for a while, and if they become loose or come undone, tie them securely with another thread.
si demorrait et servira ensi tout son tens, et c’est li forme des dens et li figure de l’adrecement des II dens sains, et des II meus, si com tu vois:	 if it is still and serves its purpose well, this is how the bones are shaped and their outline is made.
Et quant li dent chiet, si lou remet on en son leu, de fres en fres, si com nos avons dit;	 And when the tooth becomes loose, then they remove it in its place, one by one, as we have said.
et ne s’en entremette mie qui n’est saiges et soffrans, et aucune fois fait on la forme d’un dent d’os de vaiche, et lou met on au leu ou li defaute est, et l’estraint on si com nos avons dit, et demore et sert ensi lonc tens.	 and they do not get tired of removing it from its place or causing harm to the shape of a healthy tooth until it is removed as we have said, so that it does not move at all times.
de coper lou liien de la lengue	 And if you want to know
Aucune fois est cist liiens qui vient desoz la lengue ou naturez, que on naist ensi;	 "No creature comes from earth or nature itself, except [this one].
ou par accident de plaie soudee;	 "Or by a wound's sudden blow.
et li ovraiges est telz que tu oevre la bouche dou malaide, et ait sa teste en ton sain, et li lieve la lengue;	 "The ulcers are so severe that you should open your mouth and let the sores touch your tongue, but not bite it.
puis cope lou liien nervous dou large, tant que li lengue soit desloie de son tenement, et se il i a duresce ou nout, et c’est de soudement de plaie, si i boute l’uncine et cope dou large celui liement;	 "Then cure the ulcers gently and steadily as the tongue loosens its hold on it, until they are healed or ulcerated. If you bite them, immediately cover with something soft.

li chapistres des apostemes	 physicians

Et li seconde maniere si est por les leus ou il sont au cors.	 The second way is to cut into veins located at the wrist.
car li apostemes dou chief est autres que cil dou fondement, et li apostemes dou leu charnut est autres que cil qui vient en jointures, et chescuns ait son jugement en l’uevre.	 Because of their different foundations and purposes, the two types of physicians differ in terms of judgment; one is experienced through practice while the other gains experience from observation.

When physicians operate on joints, they let it rest until the wound is healed and as long as the tendons of the joint are torn, because this causes contraction in that member.

dou fremit	 This sentence does not have a clear meaning

de la forme dou clistere	 Of the fire cautery

Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	 The form of fire cautery is as follows:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez;	 If there is a danger or the veins are blocked, as you see it and try to treat it without delay;

des plaies	 wounds

Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans, et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut:	 "I tell you that when a simple wound comes or severe one, and it is not broken, if you gently touch the base of it, your finger will hold steady until the wound heals.

de la plaie dou col	 Of the wound two columns
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	 The wound comes and it is simple, if there is no difference between the two columns but if the artery has been cut.

de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	 of a burn wound

saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	 when the wound becomes mortal.

s’elle est grans, de cousture;	 If it's large, then bandaging is necessary.

si te tien dou coper.	 If you are uncertain about it.

In that case, it's recommended to first correct the dislocation at its base repeatedly and then apply pressure to stabilize the joint as much as possible, followed by treating it until it becomes stable
Li soudemens que vient as dois ensamble vient par naissance, ou par soudement de plaie, ou par arsure de feu, ou par semblans choses.	 The neighbors come together through birth or injury, or the result of fire, or similar things.
Si couvient que tu copes celle soudeure, si que li doit repairent selonc lor formes naturelz;	 If it is convenient to treat that sore place in the way of its natural shape:
puis met entre dous tentes ou drapelz moilliez en oile roset, qu’il ne se soudent;	 And let it lie still.
ou tu met entre dous pieces de plonc subtilz, tant que li leus soit soudez, si com il covient.	 Or, you can put something like this: "Or, place a thin strip of cloth between two slippery surfaces as long as they are smooth; if necessary.
Se soudemens vient a aucun de ses dois avec la paume, si cope celle sodure si com il covient.	 If the neighbors come together with only one hand, then apply pressure to the dislocated shoulder as much as possible.
des vils	 The bad ones
Vis sont voinnes grosses envoloupees pleines de superfluitez melancoliouses, que vienent em plusors membres dou cors;	 If the veins swell with melancholy-filled fluids and come to fill both arms;
et plus avient en jambes de ces qui vont a piet et qui travaillent et portent, que a autres.	 And for those that go upwards to the feet and work and carry things; others also.
Il covient donques que tu li aministres aucune fois espurgement de cole, et puis le saine de la basilique.	 It is important that you do not give any enemas without consulting a doctor first, and then wash the stomach lining afterwards.
Li cure de fer si est selonc II manieres:	 The treatment of fire is done in two ways
l’une est c’on les cope, et traie on fuer le sanc noir;	 One way is to burn the abscess and drain the black pus;
et li autre maniere si est que tu lieves la voinne, et la trai toute fuer.	 The other method is to tie off the vein tightly so as to stop the flow of blood;
Li taille si est selonc ceste maniere:	 Cutting is done in two ways:
arose li premier la jambe d’aigue chaude mout fort, tant que li gros sans soit subtiliiez, puis estrain la jambe dou malaide des desus la cuixe jusc’a la partie desoz le genoil;	 First cut the arm of a very hot person deeply so that no hair is left, and then sew up the wound at its base near to where the elbow joins it.
puis cope la voinne en I leu, ou en II ou en III, d’une taille large, puis eslieve et trair fuer le sanc noir a ta main, des l’un chief jusc’a l’autre, tant que tant de sans en isse com li vertus dou malaide puet soffrir;	 Then apply the wound with black soot to one hand, and then to the other, as much as possible from each side of the abscess, so that it may heal quickly.
et puis la lie, et li comande qu’il se teigne de viandes enjanrant cole noire;	 Then tie a black ribbon around his neck to keep him quiet while you attend to him
et recomence l’evacuation et la sainie quant les voinnes sont plainnes, et nuist au malaide.	 And start the evacuation and healing process once veins are clear, and no longer apply any medication.
Li alevemens de li est selonc ceste maniere:	 The attendants will do it as follows
reis la jambe dou malaide, s’il i a mout de poil, puis le met ou bain, et li arose la jambe d’aigue chaude tant qu’elle deviegne rouge, et enflent les voinnes;	 Stretch the leg with an abscess if there is some hair growth, and then submerge it in hot water until it turns red, and heat the veins.
et se tu n’as point de baing, si le chaufe au feu, et puis le cope endroit la voinne dou lonc au chief dou genoil, ou en la partie desoz a la cheville;	 If there is no boil at the fire's end, and then you apply the cautery to the vein near its base with the same mixture of soot or from the part towards the shoulder.
puis aoevre le cuir a l’oncine, et escorche la voinne de chescune part, tant qu’ele apere quant on la sent;	 As you apply heat to the skin, gently cleanse the affected area as much as possible.
et on la voit rouge et noire, et quant elle entre ou cuir si semble ausi com une corde blainche;	 It turns red and black, like a bruise turning white
puis boute le rait desoz, tant qu’ele soit alevee dou cuir, et puis la pent a l’oncine legier, puis le cope en I autre leu ensus III dois;	 Then apply the ointment, keeping it level on the skin, and then gently press at the affected point with three fingers.
puis escorche le cuir sus la voinne tant qu’ele apere, puis la lieve au rais, si com tu as fait, et la pent a un autre uncine, si com tu as fait premiers;	 Then gently cleanse the skin at the affected point until it stops, and then apply cool compresses if you have done so already, and press on another part just like before.
puis cope une autre taille, ou plusors se tu en as mestier, puis la lieve, et la cope au doi dou piet, puis la trai et lieve jusc’a la seconde taille;	 Then apply another piece, or more if you have more, and gently press it at the second point, then remove and cool just like before.
puis l’estrai de taille en taille, tant qu’elle isse toute fuer, puis la cope;	 Then take off each piece in turn until all are removed, and press on.
et se tu ne la pues traire et lever, si i boute une aguille a tout I fil fort double, et la lie et la trai, et i boute desoz I rait, et torne ta main d’une part et d’autre, tant qu’il en isse;	 And if you cannot remove and press as described above, prick the whole thread with two needles very strongly, then tie it tightly and cut off that hand.
et garde qu’elle ne cope, car s’elle cope, si ne la puet on traire ne lever, et en vient nuisement au malaide;	 "And let it remain still, for if it moves at all, you cannot hold or lift it, and when that happens there is great harm.
et quant tu l’as toute traite, si met sor le leu de la plaie laine moillie en vin et en oile roset;	 "And once the wound has been treated, if you apply a mixture of fine wine and oil to the healing area.
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 "And it should be applied until it is healed.
Et se li vis est contraite et torte et envoloupee ensamble, et ele n’est mie droite, si com nos avons dit, si covient que tu la fendes tortement, mais ne la coper mie;	 "And if the veins are contorted and torn, and the skin is torn together with them, but it does not move straight away as we have said, then you must stretch it gently but do not pull it straight.
et la trai si com nos avons devant dit.	 "As long as what has been mentioned previously remains unchanged.
Li forme dou fer dont on cope la vis si est corbes, et ne trenche mie, qu’il ne cope la voinne;	 "The form of the fire that is applied to the vein should be burned without any interruption so as not to cut through the vein.
et est de grosse corbeure, car s’il estoit subtilz, si coperoit la voine, mais soit gros si com nos avons dit, et ci est li forme:	 "And it is a large burn because if it were subtle, then you would have burned through the vein. But rather, as we mentioned earlier and this is how it should be done.
de la voinne civile	 "from the civil vein
Ceste voinne est enjanree en jambes, en chaudes parties ou il ne naist herbes ne arbre, et en terre ou il n’a point de moistor;	 This sentence means "This vein is straight through legs, without branches or roots, in the earth where there is no moisture.
et par aventure naist autre part qu’en jambes, et ceu avient de la porriture que vient desoz le cuir, si com il vient dedens le cors serpens et vers, enjanrez entre cuir et char.	 And on the other hand, there is another part that occurs in the legs and it comes from a source near the skin if you go between the skin and the fur;
Et se li signes de l’encomencement de ceste voinne si est qu’il vient en la jambe une tres grans enflammation, puis se chainge li leus, et comence li voinne fors issir, ausi com une racine d’une plante.	 And when the beginning of this vein becomes inflamed and begins to swell, and as if a root of a plant is growing

et s’elle est trop longe, si en cope une partie, et envoloupe le remenant, et ne la coper mie en sa racine, tant qu’elle soit toute issue;	 If too long, if you cut a part of it off and wrap the remaining around your finger, and do not put it back on until both ends are together.
car se tu la copes, si rentre en la char, et fait venir aposteme et porriture ou leu, et male maladie;	 Because if you cut through it, it will enter into the artery or vein and cause harm to the body.

et soit vuidie li matiere qui est dedens, et amenistre au leu medicines enjanrans porriture aucun jor, puis le cure si com les apostemes.	 And when dealing with materials that are dense or heavy, apply the treatment to the affected area and use gentle medications in order not to cause any harm, then treat as you would an abscess.

cure le donques si com nos avons dit devant.	 Treat as you would have previously advised.
des vers qui naissent entre cuir et char	 Between flesh and bone
Ceste maladie est apelee en nostre terre «maladie de buef», por ceu qu’elle avient maintes fois as bués, et est un petis vers qui naist entre cuir et char, et va par tout le cors montant et dessendant, et le sent om bien a l’aler de membre en membre, tant qu’il desront le cuir ou il vait, et saut fuer;	 This illness is known in our land as "flesh disease," because it often appears between the skin and bone, and moves up and down through every part of the body, causing pain to each member equally until they touch the skin or it retreats.
et est enjanrez de porriture d’aucunes humors, si com vienent vers et serpens et lumbris et ascarides ou ventre;	 And there are discharges of certain humours, whether they come from wounds or burns or bruises or abscesses in the belly.
et doute on de son malice, car quant il va par le cors, et il monte au chief, et il vient a l’oil, par aventure rentre, et destruit l’oil;	 And doubts arise about its evil influence because when it passes through the body and rises to the head, it comes back down in oil form, destroying the oils.
et ceu avient maintes fois.	 This often happens.
Quant tu le vues curer et traire, si ne puet on fuers que quant il vait:	 When you cure and bind it tightly, if not done properly will cause the patient to become worse as time goes on.
si covient donques que tu lies le leu desus et desoz d’un fort liien bien estroitement, puis cope sus et le trai fuer, et se li vers est em parfont en la char, et tu ne le trueves, si le cauterize de feu sus, tant qu’il muire;	 When you loosen the ends of a thick and straight thread, then tie it tightly in its own loop, and do not remove it until it burns to the bone.
et li plus grans nuisemens que il fait, si est qu’il corront l’oil, si com nos avons dit;	 And there are more serious damages that occur when oil comes out of them, as we have mentioned earlier.

de la dolor qui vient de ventositeit	 Of the pain that comes from ventsite
Ceste maladie est apelee en nostre terre «vakirir», et est une dolor que vient en aucuns membres, et pues se mue de membre en membre;	 This disease is called "waker" in our land and it comes to any member of the body, causing them to move around like a snake.
et je vis ceu que je vos di.	 I understand that you want me to do this too.
Je fui apelez a une femme malaide, et me descovrit som bras, et vis une petite enfleure en la voinne dou brais;	 I called upon a female healer and she revealed in my hands, and saw a small tumor on the vein of both arms.
et I poc aprés, li vis monter ausi com un ver a l’espaule, plus tost que nulle chose, ausi com vif argent quant il cort de leu a autre;	 And afterwards, it grew like a thorn in my shoulder, more quickly than nothing, as if made of silver when I cut through the vein.
li dolor se departit de celui leu, et se ficha en l’espaule, et puis un poc aprés corrut par tout le cors, tant qu’ele vint en l’autre brais;	 The pain left my arm and settled in my shoulder, then spread throughout the body, reaching to the other arm.
puis me contait qu’elle tornioit adés entor le cors, si com je la vis.	 She told me that she would tear apart the body if I continued like this.
Je me mervillai mout coment elle se movoit ensi de membre em membre, car je n’avoie onques veut ceste maladie selonc ceste maniere.	 I was amazed at how it spread from joint to joint because I had never seen such a disease spread in this way before.
Toutevoie, je avoie veut maint que bien avoient veut movoir dolor de leu a autre, mais je ne l’avoie mie veut, si com je le vis en la femme;	 For every ailment I've ever encountered, except for this one here that you mentioned, but I cannot help if I see it in her.
et je me pensai que c’estoit por ceu que li femme avoit sec cors, et les voinnes descovertes, et por ceu apparoit celle ventositez constrainte;	 I thought this was because the woman had a weak heart and veins were exposed, which seemed to put pressure on her chest.
et n’aperent mie selonc ceste raison a ces qui sont delicious, et qui ont moistes cors et voinnes reponues.	 But they didn't seem to notice that as the reason for these who are healthy and have plump veins.

et cauterize le leu;	 Cauterize her arm.

des saiettes	 arrows
Les saiettes sont diverses, selonc lor semblances et selonc les leus dou cors ou elles chient.	 Arrows are various depending on their likeness and where they enter the body.
Li diversitez de lor si est qu’il i a de celles qui ont grans pointes, et petites, et chevees, et soudees;	 The limbs are diverse because they have different lengths, sizes, shapes, and qualities.
et de celles qui ont II angles, et de celz qui ont lengues, et de celles ou il a pieces;	 And those that have two ends or two points of the same length, like fingers and toes,

ou en membre principeil cheveit, si com cerveil, cuer, foie, pormon, rains, intestine, vessie, et semblans membres.	 Or on the principle of a single body part, such as the arm or leg, if necessary, but otherwise all members.
Quant elle chiet donques en aucun leu de ces membres, et li signe de mort, que je te dirai ci aprés, t’aperent:	 When she is dislocated without any of these parts and the sign of death will be told to you later on, pay attention.

saiches adonc sens doute ke li mors dessent.	 "Many are likely to die.

The sign of the sixth day is when no relief can be felt from the itch and swelling of sores; the throat swells up, and the hairs turn white and cold; those who doubt will die.

et li muevent tuit li membre des espaules.	 and the limb moves out of place.

saiches que li plaie est mortelz.	 The wound has become mortal.
Li autre membre, si com li faice et li colz et li gorge et li espaule et li adjutoire et li espinee dou dos et li forcele et li cuixe et les jambes, et li membre semblant, sont sauf selonc plusors dispositions. When the arrow enters into a nerve or artery and does not enter immediately, as you may ask me to explain what I mean by this, that is, unless otherwise specified
Il avint a I home c’une saiette li chut ou larmier en la racine dou neis:	 He found it at the root of his nose, causing him to bleed badly from there.
je la tentai, et la traï d’autre part desoz la graisse de l’oreille, et fut sanez sens nusement.	 I tried this, and was blinded by the fat in the ear and became insane as a result.

et mout d’autres semblans.	 similar things (dislocations).

et il le me dist.	 It is reset (or: "put back" or "made whole again").

et trespassa bien li termines entor IIII mois, et puis eslarja si li plaie que je i boutai les tenailles, et le meus d’une part et d’autre, et ne pot issir;	 And afterwards bind the wound with four ropes for four months, and then tie them tightly on both sides to prevent any escape.

mais li saiges maistres compere sus bien poc grant chose, et sus ceu que li est present et defaillant, trueve nueve oevre, et nuef estrument, au dessendement des choses estrainges qui avienent en cest art.	 But the master of the course will not approve or follow this strange and dangerous method that involves harmful things
Je dis que les saiettes n’issent des membres ou elles sont fichies fuer que selonc II manieres:	 I say that arrows do not enter into any member unless they are guided in one of these ways.
ou par lou leu ou elles entrent, ou par d’autre part;	 Or through the left side or through another way.
et celle que saut fuer par lai ou elle entre, c’est saiette entrans en leus charnus, et saut fuer aucune fois maintenant.	 The one that passes by the left side enters into the lung and never again;
Et s’elle ne saut maintenant, si la laisse tant que li chars soit porrie entor, et soit alegie li issue;	 If she does not pass now if she is allowed to stay with her hair standing up and without any obstruction in its path.
et ausi s’elle est fichie en l’os, et elle ne puet issir, si la laisse ensi aucuns jors, et la muef chescun jor;	 And if it is fixed into the bone, then it cannot move unless you loosen it a little.
et adonques elle saut, et s’elle ne saut, si perce entor a tout I foret subtil, tant que li leus entor soit eslargiez, et puis la trai.	 And when it jumps and does not jump, if you gently pull on the edge with great force, then stretch it out slowly.

Et se li saiette n’est fichie fuer qu’en l’os soulement, et ne vient jusc’a syfac, et demoure li malaides aucuns jors sens mavais accident, si l’engigne dou traire.	 And the dislocation only occurred in that bone and does not occur elsewhere, leading to serious injury if it occurs without holding steady; it's important to keep it still for a moment or two.

puis cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	 then treat the wound while it is bleeding.

La qualitez de la sainie si est selonc ta pensee.	 The quality of the vein is as follows:
Li premiere chose que tu dois savoir de sainier, si est que sainie n’est amenistree fuer que por garder santeit, et por eschuir les maladies a venir;	 The first thing you should know when healing from surgery is that recovery will take time to ensure health and prevent future complications.
et soit li sainie faite en l’une des III voinnes que sont ou coute:	 And if the operation was done on one of the three veins mentioned below;

et se doit on sainier en l’encomencement de prientens a geun, et en autompne et en yver aprés mengier, quant li signe de repletion aperent;	 And when it is necessary to start feeding them again after weaning, and gradually increase their intake as they grow older.
et se doit on sainier le premier jor ou le tier, aprés II houres ou III dou jor.	 Feed them the first time in the morning or afternoon; wait two hours or three hours later to feed again.

et s’il aoevre la voinne, si est li plaie trop estroite, por ceu si covient que li sainieres soit avisez en ces choses.	 And if their hand swells excessively due to a too severe burn, then they should seek medical attention immediately in these situations.

et ceu meisme fait triaicle et bowe d’eus, quant on le met sus le leu;	 "And when it is placed back onto its place.
si subtilie li sans et s’espart quant il est trop gros.	 It becomes too heavy and splits apart if there's too much weight put upon it.

Li sainie de la sophene si vaut a toutes les maladies que sont desoz le cors, si com maladies de la marris, et retenement de flors, et maladie des rains, et des cuixes et des jambes ancienes, et semblans maladies. Li leus de la voinne sciatique est a la cheville de fuer, et sa sainie vaut a la dolor de la hainche, quant c’est por sanc chaut.	 Sciatic vein pain is in the calf and shoulder area, and it's often caused by inflammation.

des sainies de ventouse	 The veins
Ventouses sont fait de cornes, ou d’arain, ou de voirre;	 "The veins are cut through bone or sinew;
et ventosation si est faite selonc II manieres:	 "...and the extraction is made in two ways:
ou par ferir et atraire sanc, ou sens ferir.	 "Or by cutting and drawing out the vein, or piercing.
Et ceste ventosation qui est sens ferir si est selonc II manieres:	 "...the extraction made by piercing is done in two ways:
ou elle est a tout feu, ou sens feu;	 "Either it is heated up or the heat is applied;
et ventosation qui est faite par ferir et par estraction de sanc si est faite en XIIII leus dou cors, de coi li uns est tout en som le chief;	 "And separation which is made by cutting or extraction of abscesses should be done in four pieces to prevent the joint from being dislocated.
et li autres est emmi le col;	 "And other separations are made through the neck.
et II autres en II costeis dou col;	 "The second separation is made through two holes in the neck.
et li ventouse desoz lou menton;	 "And the exit of the abscesses from the nose.
et li ventouse des II espaules;	 "And the exit of the second space.
et li ventouse sus les crupies;	 "And the exit of the sores.
et les ventouses emmi les II bras;	 "The exits are made through both arms.
et les ventouses des II jambes;	 "The exits are made through both legs.
et les ventouses des II chevilles;	 "The exits are made through the two heels.
et li ventosation ne trait point de sanc, fuer que des menues voinnes que sont esparses en la char, et por ceu n’en afoiblist om mie, si com on fait de sainie de voinne;	 "The separation cannot treat abscesses that are sparse in the cloth, and therefore it is not forbidden to do the same with veins.
et ne covient mie qu’elle soit aministree, ne a tout feu ne sens feu, en aucune maladie qui vient de repletion, tant que toz li cors soit vuidiez.	 "It should be used only for a short time and does not cause any harm, in no illness that comes from excess, as long as the skin is healed.
Et se par necessiteit de maladies covient ventoser, ou por acostumances, si l’amenistrons chescune houre en l’encomencement dou mois, ou en la fin, et emmi et en chescun tens;	 And it is necessary to perform these procedures either before or after the month has ended, at dawn and in the evening, every day until you finish.
car il i a de telz qui, quant il ont mestier de ventoser, si ont pesant chief;	 because when one knows how to sew properly, if he is patient enough;
et si a telz qui truevent repletion et roujor en lor faice, et en lor chief, et au col, et tenebrour as eulz;	 and if the fire gets too hot in their face or head, or at the ears, and blind them.

Li sainie de la muze si aide a la grieteit dou chief … que vient as eulz, et ne covient mie que ce soit aprés l’evacuation de tout lou cors;	 The patient who receives help with the fire treatment... which comes after the evacuation of all the limbs.
et ceste ventosation si est en leu de la sainie de la cephalique, et ne covient mie que cil qui est de froide complexion en use, ou qui ait chatharre, car ce lor fait mout grant nuisement;	 and this evacuation should be in the absence of a cerebral stroke, or those with a cold constitution should avoid it, as it causes great harm.
et por ceu ne covient mie que li veillart en usent, ne qui ont ou chief froides maladies.	 And because he is to cover it with ice
Et cil qui s’en saine sovent, si devient oblious, et por ce covient mettre la ventouse un poc plus aval par la doutance d’obliance.	 And those who are well advised to do so should place their head slightly lower in order to prevent dislocation
Li ventosation emmi le col est en leu de la sainie dou chief et de la basilique, et por ceu vaut elle a l’estrecement dou pis, et a fendure de la chenal dou pormon, et a toust, et a repletion;	 He is vomiting because of the severity and depth of injury in his chest and abdomen.
et la covient poc bouter, car s’elle tient trop fermement, si enjanre obliance ou stomac et ou cuer.	 And it's important to breathe slowly but deeply if she holds her breath too long, as this may cause damage to the esophagus or stomach
Li ventosations as II costelz dou col si vaut as dolors dou chief, et obtalmie et emigrainne, et a l’estranglement, et a la dolor as racines des dens, et est en leu de la sainie de la basilique;	 The vomiting is severe and painful in the chest, causing constriction of the esophagus, and may cause damage to the intestines.
et covient que tu comandes au sainor qu’il espresse sa main au mettre, qu’il ne cope l’artere, et ne veigne decorremens de sanc.	 It is important that he commands his stomach to release and hold off on vomiting, not covering the artery, so as not to cause damage from bleeding.

et est en leu des sainies des II levres.	 And it is from this level of veins.
Li ventosations des espaules vaut a maladie que vient de chalor et de remplissement.	 The dislocations of joints are an illness caused by heat and swelling.
Li ventosations des coutes si vaut autant com des III voinnes dou bras, car elle atrait sanc de ces grosses voinnes;	 Dissections are as dangerous as those in the upper arm because they cut through large veins.

et par aventure, s’elle estoit subtilz, si briseroit;	 And if they are subtle, there would be a rupture.
et i fai grans plaies.	 This could result in large wounds.
Les ventouses des jambes si sainent apertement, car elles atraient sanc de tout le cors, et valent as dolors ancienes des rains, et de la marris, et de la vessie, et ramoinnent les flors;	 Dissections of the legs should not be done too quickly because they can cut through all of your veins and arteries, causing severe pain from the neck down to the feet.
et sont en leu des II sophenes, et des II chevilles, et toutevoie elles afoiblissent lou cors aprés lonc us, et font venir paumison em plusors dispositions.	 They are in the area of the second vein and second calf, causing them to weaken your body after a long time, leading to fainting spells more often.
Li maniere de mettre la ventouse si est que tu la mettes premier vuide, et succe tempreement, et la met hastanment, et remue igalment, et ne cesser de ceu faire, tant que tu voies lou leu rouge et enfleit, et apere li roujor dou sanc;	 Here is the translation: The method to apply a bandage is to put it on first as quickly and smoothly as possible, and then fasten it firmly, and remove it gently, repeating this process continuously until you reach your target color of red and fade out.
puis fier, et remet les ventouses, et pren warde en la disposition des cors, car il i a telz qui ont tanre char, et clers porez:	 Then after that, apply more bandages and take care to arrange them properly on the body because they are essential for support; in particular for wounds.
si covient ferir une fois soulement, et covient faire larges plaies, et un poc parfondes;	 If you only want one bandage then make sure it's wide enough to cover a large area or many small ones.
et suce legierement.	 And gently squeeze them in place.
Et se li sans est gros, si couvient ferir II fois:	 If the first bandage is not strong enough then you should apply another one as well.
la premiere fois por subtiliier la voie dou sanc gros.	 The first time to make it smaller and tighter around the wound.
Et se li sans est tres espés, si covient ferir la tierce fois;	 If the second bandage is still not strong enough then apply another one as well.
et quant nos volons traire dou sanc poc et poc, si nos soffist soulement une fois.	 And when we want to draw out a small piece at a time and only once if we simply use one bandage.
Et se nos volons mout de sanc, si rencomensons sovent;	 And if we want to cure the illness, then let's begin.
et se li sans est espés, si fier em parfont, et li termines si est que li keurs soit perciez soudement, et couvient a celui qui a gros cuir et dur, et qui ont estrois porelz, que tu oignes les leus des ventouses d’oile aperitif et dissolutif:	 And if his heart is strong and steady, then let's begin.
se c’est en esteit, d’oile violet, ou d’oile d’amandres douces, ou d’oile de semence de cucurbite;	 It could be with rose oil or almond oil, or seed of cucumber oil;
et se c’est en yveir, d’oile de cresson, ou de lis, ou de camomille, ou autre semblant.	 Or if it is from lavender oil, or lilies, or chamomile, or any similar oil.
Et se li superfluitez est grosse et froide, si pren oile amaratin, ou de balsamite, ou oile d’anet, et les semblans.	 "And if you apply excessive amounts of fat, cold, or oil-based substances such as balsamite, or other oils which may freeze,
Et se cil cui on saine a tendre char et larges porelz, se n’i covient mettre point d’oile, mais le covient laver aprés la ventosation d’aigue rose, ou d’aigue froide, ou d’aigue de morelle, ou d’aigue de cucurbite, ou d’aigue de porcelainne, ou autre semblant.	 "And when you apply a soothing char and wide pores, it is not advisable to put oil on them; instead, wash after applying cold or hot water, or egg yolk, or mullein, or porcelain, or similar substances.
Et cil qui a mout de moistor, si se leve d’aisil, ou d’aigue de mirte, et de sumac, et de semblans choses.	 "And those who have issues with moisture, such as itching, or abscesses, and similar things.
Et cil qui ont grosses superfluitez se levent de vin viel, ou d’aigue de seuc, ou de decoction d’anet ou de camomile, ou d’autres semblans;	 Those with excessive fluids may be treated with wine vinegar or sweet vinegar, or a tea of anise or chamomile, or others.
et ne se covient mie sainier de ventouse devant le bain ne em bain, mais aprés lou bain une houre ou II;	 Do not sit in the bath before washing it off, but after washing it off wait one to two hours;
et ne dorme mie aprés la ventosacion, et covient k’il se warse, quant il se doit ventoser et quant il est ventosez.	 Do not sleep right away afterwards, and you must rest when you should shave, as well as when it is shaved off.
Et warde se cil qui se saine est coleriques, et se li sans est trop agus et enflamez;	 And beware of those who are colic (suffering from) colic, and whose anus is too inflamed.
si covient qu’il preigne choses froides, si com pomes grenates et endives et laitues a l’aisil, et semblans choses;	 If it's advisable to eat cold foods, such as spinach, lettuce and cucumber, among others.
et menjuce pucins, et char de chastron, et viandes moistes.	 And drink ale (beer)
Et cil qui a froide complexion, si preigne syrop de miel, et vin odorant moien, qui est entre viel et noveil, et menjuce poc, et menjuce pucins et petis oiselz et pijons;	 And those with a cold complexion should drink honey syrup and musty wine which is between old and new, eat some food, eat bread, cheese, oil, fish, eggs, and poultry.
et lou jor qu’il se ventousera, si doit plus boivre que mengier;	 And those who are about to vomit should drink more than they eat (to prevent vomiting).
et covient doner a aucuns homes aucune fois triaicle ou muscate devant la ventosacion, ou aprés, por conforter les membres principalz;	 And it is advisable not to scratch or itch in front of the mirror when you are about to vomit, or afterwards, so as to maintain the alignment of the limbs.
et soit subtiliiez li sans, mais il ne covient mie que cil qui sont chaut le boivent.	 And be gentle with those who are hungry, but do not advise those who are already full.
Les ventouses que sont mises sens ferir sont celles que sont mises sus lou foie, et sus la mice, et podagre, et sus lou ventre et la boude et les rains et la hainche, car cil membre ne soffrent mie ferir sus oulz, et ne le fait on fuer que por atraire sanc de membre em membre, si com nos mettons sus les mameles quant li neis sainne;	 The wounds that are being made to bleed are those that have been placed upon the liver and spleen, and abdomen, and buttocks and thighs and head and neck, because this member cannot withstand the stabbing of another part of the body, nor will it occur if one tries to stab a wound from a wound on the same side;
por oster la viscositeit qui est au membre, si com nos metons ventouses sus le ventre et sus la boude por amenuisier le membre;	 Because of the viscosity inside the member, as we place wounds upon the belly and buttocks to hinder movement.
et oste la dolor, quant il i a opilation ou piere, si oste par sa vertu atractive par aventure l’opilation, ou desaert la piere de son leu;	 And pain when it has an ulcer or stone, either by its attractive nature to attract the extraction, or by removing the source of the ulcer.
et ensi fait ele quant on le met sus lou foie et sus la mice quant il i a ventositeit retenue, et ces ventouses sont aministrees vuides por sucier tant soulement;	 And it is done when we place upon the liver and spleen as they retain the moisture only.
et aucune fois sont aministrees ensamble feu, et aucunes fois plainnes d’aigue tede, si com em maladies dou pleuresin, et en tel maniere c’on emplisse la ventouse d’aigue chaude soule, ou d’aigue ou il ait cuit herbes covenaubles a ceu.	 It is always done together with fire, and never alone unless it has been burned for herbs, or to remove stones in that way.
Li forme de la ventouse aministré a feu si est ci:	 The form of venesection (venipuncture) administered is as follows:
Et ait II dois de large et demi palme de parfont, et ait ou costeit entor lou mileu I petit pertus, ausi com por bouter une aguille, et soit d’arain, souef devant si qu’ele ne blece lou malaide au mettre sus lou membre;	 And the patient must put his hand wide and half palm forward, so that it may strike a thorn without fear, or of rain, for if he does not hold back from striking at an arrow,
et ait em mileu une verge de travers d’arain ou de fer, por mettre une chandoile emprise, et en soient et grans et petites selonc les maladies et l’eaige de ces qui les prenent;	 and in cases of injury by fire or iron, for putting a tourniquet on, and there are large and small according to the severity and nature of those who take them.
car les ventouses des enfans sont autres que des vielz, et des maigres que des gras.	 as the veins of children are different from adults, and thin ones from fat ones.
Et doit on ensi mettre ceste ventouse sus lou membre:	 And so it is necessary to put this tourniquet on the limb
empren la chandoile de cire ou I linement, et le met emmi la ventouse au traver de la verge qui est emmi la ventouse, si que li clartez soit au fons de la ventouse qu’elle ne brule le malaide;	 by using either a tourniquet made of linen or another material, and place it around the vein at its furthest point away from where you want to apply pressure.
et puis la met sus lou membre, et tes dois soit sus lou pertus que nos avons dit, si que quant on vuet, si en va li vapor, et oste on la ventouse;	 and then place it around the limb, making sure that where you apply pressure matches what we've said, if when you see it, or its gone wrong, and remove it.
et emprent on le linement si com devant, et le rencomence sovent, se tu as mestier.	 "And fasten it down firmly while facing forward, and repeat until you feel sore.
En la ventouse donques qui est aministree em maladie de pleuresin, a tout aigue, n’a point de verge ne de pertus, et n’est amenistree fuer que quant ele est plaine d’aigue, et est mise sus lou membre tant soulement;	 "In the treatment of pleurisy where there is often no coughing or difficulty in breathing, and it is mild only when the chest is opened up gently, and held only on one side.
et c’est li forme:	 "This means:
Sansues ne sont amenistrees fuer que en membres ou on ne puet mettre ventouses por lour petitece, si com levres et gencives, et semblans leus;	 "No stitches are necessary if there is no difficulty breathing in the body parts or when ventilating them gently and smoothly.
et en leus desnuez de char, si com doi ou neis, et autres semblans;	 "And in the eyes you must close them tightly so they do not move until they grow.
et li qualitez de l’user si est que quant tu trueves sansues que sont en aigues douces nettes sens porreture, si les pren;	 "The quality of the user is that whenever you remove stitches which are soft and neat from the opening, if they are pricked.
et les met une nut en aigue douce, tant qu’elles soient famillouses, et n’aient rien en ventres;	 "And after removal hold them gently until they become closed up tightly without any leakage anywhere.
et puis soit sainiez de voinne et de ventouse, puis frote le membre tant k’il soit rouges, et met sus les sansues;	 "And please hold down the arm and wrist until it is red.
et quant elles seront plainnes, et cherront, se c’est leu ou on puisse mettre ventouse, se li met, car ce vaut mout aprés.	 And when they are smooth and hard, you may then apply pressure, as this is recommended afterwards.
Se ceu non, si leve le leu d’aisil, et puis d’aigue, mout bien, et puis l’espreint;	 If not, if the joint becomes loose again, gently stretch it and hold for a moment to release tension.
et se li leus saine trop aprés lou cors des sansues, si moille I drapel de lin en aigue froide, et met sus, tant que li sans soit estenchiés;	 And if the joint becomes too loose after an extended stretch in cold water, gently squeeze it and hold until it is fixed.
et se li sans est multipliez, si met sus vitriole broié, ou gales, et semblans choses, tant qu’il soit estenchiez;	 And if the joint becomes swollen or inflamed due to bruising, or from swelling and similar things, hold it fixed until it stabilizes.
ou tu met sor le leu moitiez de feves pelees, et les laisse tant qu’elles s’aerdent au leu, si estanchera maintenant;	 Or if you put heat on the joint as it becomes stiff and releases tension over time until it has completely released.
et se tu en as de plus mestier, si pren autres sansues.	 And if you have a second injury to your joint.
Et se les sansues ne se vuellent prendre, si frote le leu de sanc fres, ou tu i fiche une aguille tant que li sans en isse, et puis les met sus, et tantost com elles sentent lou sanc, si s’aerdent;	 "When the veins are pricked and cause bleeding, hold down the affected area to prevent further injury.
et quant tu vues qu’elles chieent, si poudre sus un poc d’aloen et de seil broiet, ou de cendre, si cherront maintenant.	 "When the hairs prick at their base, either hold them down gently or tie a strip around to prevent further injury.
Ci comence li livre des brisures	 The book begins with an introduction about injuries
Cist chapistres est maintes fois necessaires en l’art de medicine, et est restorement de brisure et de desaluement.	 Injuries are often necessary in the art of medicine and their healing is restoration.
Saichiez, chier fil, que li fol mire se gietent de cest chapistre, qu’il ne virent onques nul des anciens livres, ne lettre n’en lurent;	 "When the patient receives this treatment for the first time and does not find anything in any of their previous books or letters.
et por ceste cause est estraingie li science en nostre terre, car je n’en trovai onques nul boin;	 "This is also strange to us here because we found nothing related in our own works.
et n’en sai nient, fuer que par la science des anciens livres, ou j’ai tant estudiiet que je en ai traite la science, et par experiment, et par l’acostumance de ma vie;	 "I have studied and practiced medicine for a long time, through the books of my predecessors, I tried experiments myself, and by following the customs of life.
et je vos ai jai descrit en cest chapistre ceu qui est contenut, et l’ai abregié en la fin, et ai mostreit clerement les formes des estrumens que sont amenistrez, si com j’ai fait en ces II chapistres ci devant.	 "In this chapter I have described what is contained in it and laid out its contents at the end; I explicitly explained the forms of the remedies to be practiced as we do in these two preceding chapters.
Il covient donques que nos disons ou prologue de cest livre les sommes de la parole et les chapistres ou li saiges met son entendement, et demore sus la verteit, si que cil qui sont esproveit saichent et aprenent cest art noble, et l’aprenent a autrui.	 Here is the translation line by line: "The prologue of this book introduces the speakers and explains their role in it, and proceeds to teach them how to use it well, if they are skilled enough and have learned its noble art.
Je dis que quant brisure ou dislocation ou torsions ou quasseure vient a aucun, si covient que tu te hastes de sainier lou malaide d’une part et d’autre, s’aucune chose ne lou te tot, si com foiblece de cors, ou enfes, ou viellars;	 I say that if there is a break or dislocation or sprain comes from any of the joints in the body, it should be treated immediately by supporting one end and holding the other firmly, so nothing else happens, even if the limb is bent forward or backward.
ou se li tens n’est tres chaus, ou trop frois;	 or if there are excessive swelling or stiffness
et menjuce cholz frois, c’est a savoir froides joutes, et char d’oiseil et de chevril, et ne boive point de vin, ne menjuce nules grasses chars, et ne s’emplisse mie trop de viandes qui remplissent les voinnes de sanc, tant que tu n’aies doute d’aposteme chaut, ne d’espandement de matiere au membre;	 and if there is excessive swelling or stiffness, it's important to have cold compresses on the affected areas, and avoid applying heat as much as possible, do not fill your wounds with raw meat unless you are absolutely sure that this is necessary for treating the wound.
si reviegne li malaides a som premerain governement k’il a useit.	 if the hair of the affected area becomes very long and tangled, it should be trimmed gently to prevent injury.
Et quant li os brisiés comence a restourer, si covient que on norrisse le malaide de viandes que font gros norrissement, ou il ait viscositeit, si com froment cuit en aigue, et ris, et testes, et piez, et pance de vaiche, et oefz, et poissons fres, et gros vin, et semblans chose.	 And when the blisters begin to heal, if it is convenient that one narrows the vein causing large swelling, or viscosity, if accompanied by itching and redness, sores, pain, fever, and pus discharge, and in the fish flesh, and boils, and similar things occur
Car a teil norrissement se reprent mues et plus tost li brisure.	 When a part swells up very quickly, it may indicate that there is an infection present.
Et saichiez que li os brisiez des vielz et des decrepites ne se pueent mie bien reprendre ne souder selonc lor nature por la sechor des membres, ne cil ausi qui sont trop tendre, si com os de petis enfans;	 And it should be noted that broken veins and capillaries are unable to heal properly after the fact due to their nature as soft tissues. Additionally, if they are too tender themselves.
mais n’a cure, ramoinne sus l’os brisiet I gros tenrons qui s’aert et joint le membre ensamble, tant qu’il enforce si com il fut devant;	 "And it will come undone when the bone is broken or dislocated.
et ne li tot point de son oevre, et por ceu le covient norrir de grosses viandes, si com nos avons dit.	 "It should be left to heal naturally and not forced with large amounts of force as mentioned earlier.
Et saiches que les briseures sont diverses em maintes manieres.	 And that blisters come in many forms.
Car li brisure dou chief est autre que li brisure dou pis, ou de la jambe, et je vos dirai en cest chapistre toutes manieres de brisure.	 The first sentence does not translate directly into English but rather gives a clue as to the meaning of future sentences.
Car il i a brisure que vait a arvol, et autre en aguisant, si com li taille d’une penne por escrire.	 There was a dislocation that had gone too far and caused great pain when trying to straighten it as the joint size made it difficult to do so
Et si a brisure avec plaie, et brisure a tout une petite fendure.	 If there is a dislocation accompanied by an injury, or if the dislocation is very small.
Et a chescune maniere ait son engien, et son estrument propre en la restauration, selonc ceu que li remembrance vient en son leu;	 And that way the engine was repaired properly and its instrument cleaned according to what it had instructed.
et est conue li brisure de l’os par ceu que li leus est tors, et apert bien par defuer, et sone au presseir de la main;	 "And when a bone is broken then the process of healing begins and if it is properly treated with force.
et quant il n’i a tortuositeit ne son au tochier, et li malaides ne sent mie grant dolor, se n’i a point de brisure;	 "And when there is no twisting or misalignment of the bones and the patient experiences little to no pain, then there will be no break.
mais il puet bien avoir tortuositeit, ou fendure, ou petite brisure.	 "However, even though healing can still occur with slight twists or fractures but it may heal stronger than before.
Si ne covient mie que tu lou mueves a la main, mais met sus medicines que vienent ci aprés, et puis l’estraint maintenant subtilment.	 If only you move your arm now with the medicine that comes after, and then hold it gently now

et se apostemes chaulz i vient, si lou laisse aucun jor, tant que li apostemes soit apaisiez;	 "And hold your arms steady if they prick at their base.

et met le membre selonc sa figure natureil, si que quant les parties dou membre brisiet sont desevrees, si ramoinne par toz engiens les additions en lor leus au mues que tu pues, et garde que par ton ovraige ne viegne au malaide lesion ne doulor;	 "And hold the member to its natural shape as much as possible when the broken parts of a joint are healed, by making sure that your actions in healing do not cause further harm.

si la dresce bellement, et ne l’estraindre mie trop, ne presser si com font cil qui i font venir par lor ovraige aposteme chaut et contraction au membre, si com nos avons veut maintes fois. Saiches que li membre brisiet sont divers em petitece et en grandor et en forme.	 The dislocated limbs may vary in size, shape, and length.

et mollifie lou liien poc et poc, tant que tu preignes grant partie dou leu sain, puis repren I autre liien, et torne entor derechief sus lou leu brisiet;	 And gently loosen it a little at a time as you approach the greater part of its length, then release another one and repeat this process until you reach the end of the break.
puis revai a la partie desoz de la brisure, et l’estraint moienement, ne mie trop fort ne trop molement, si com nos avons dit en la premiere lieure desus;	 Then return to the part above the break and hold it gently but not too tightly nor loosely as we said in our previous answer.
puis met entre les liiens estoupes de lin ou drapelz, tant qu’il soit toz igalz, puis lie tout par desus I bendeil, et puis met tes esteles bien faites sus, s’il n’i a aposteme ou enfleure.	 When you put pressure on the eyes of a cloth or linen as long and even as possible, hold them steady until they prick at their base.
Et s’il i a enfleure ou aposteme, si met sus chose apaisant aposteme chaut, et qui oste l’enfleure, et le laisse ensi aucuns jors;	 If there is bleeding or bruising, do not press on the eye but rather leave it alone and allow any injury to heal naturally.
puis estrain sus tes esteles, et soient de moitiet d’une large cainne rese saigement, ou de fust dont on fait les clives, ou de rains de palme, et soient selonc ceste figure:	 Then hold the eyes steady and ensure they are at least as wide as a finger's breadth if possible; or from which you may see threads of cloth or veins in them, so that it is clear.
mais il covient que li estele que om met sus la brisure soit un poc plus grosse et plus large que les autres;	 But it is advisable to make the eye with which you are making the incision larger and more wide than others.
et soit ausi longe com il covient au membre de petitece ou de grandor;	 And so long as possible, just like when treating any other part of the body.
puis estraint sus les esteles ausi com tu as fait a la premiere lieure, puis lie desus un fil avenanment, si com en la premiere lieure sus la briseure;	 Then hold them steady just like you did in the previous incision and tie a thread gently around it if possible.
plus estroit est ensus, adés moins;	 In the beginning of a dislocation
et covient que li fil soient moien, ne trop gros ne trop menus, et soient de lin mol;	 And it is desirable that the bones be soft and not too hard or too soft, but at an appropriate size.
car se li fil sont gros, si com j’ai veut des oevres des folz qui font lor lieures des cordes de linement tort, et c’est grant error, car li lieure ne puet estre igal s’il est trop subtilz, et ne covient mie qu’il ait entre chescune estele moins dou doi d’espaice.	 If the bones are too large, if you want to make the wounds heal faster and it's a good thing because there will be no healing if it is too delicate, but it should have between two and two spans of space
Et se li malaides est navrez par les chiés des esteles aprés l’estrignement en leus sains, si met desoz elles estoupes de lin, ou lainne charpie, si qu’il ne se blece.	 After the dislocation has been reset and is properly aligned, if you apply heat to them after being cut or bruised, they will be still, unless there is some other cause for concern.
Quant li plaie est avec la briseure, et li keurs est rompus, je en dirai la cure ci aprés.	 If the wound is with frostbite and the ears are torn off, I will tell you the treatment after that.
Et saiches qu’il ne covient mie estraindre d’esteles toz les membres brisiez le premier jor.	 And if it's necessary to restrain those members from being separated immediately.

et vez ci la maniere des emplaustres anciiens por restorer brisure, dislocation, et torsion:	 And for the plastering of any fracture, dislocation, and torsion

des diverses manieres de brisure	 "of various ways of breaking

de la routure de la mandibule	 of opening the mouth

et met emplaustre sus, de la poudre dou moulin avec abun d’uef ou farine de sisament, aprés ceu que tu as osteit lou cerote;	 and apply plaster soaked in flour or bran meal after you have heated the cautery.

maintes fois est sanez en III semainnes.	 It is done every third time.

Et se li extensions ne t’est apareillie por mettre igal a tes mains, si le ramoine a cest estrument qui est de fer, qui a VII dois ou VIII de lonc, et li largesce est selonc la quantiteit de la plaie;	 And do not leave the extensions to move around when putting it in your hands if the instrument that is used for fire has seven or eight holes and its length is proportional to the size of the wound;
