et soit rons et un poc gros, k’il ne ploie mie a la compression sus lou membre a ton ovraige, et soit agus devant, et gros des le mileu en avant, ensi:	 And if there is not enough, he will not be able to compress the limb against its place, and may fall forward or backward depending on that.
Et est apelez «palainche», por coi il covient que li chiés corbes soit mis sus lou chief de l’os apparent;	 And the dislocation is called "Palinch," because when it occurs, there should be a fracture at or near the end of the affected bone.

et maintes fois ont ce fait li fol mire, et ont fait venir sus le malaide ou mort ou corrodent aucune fois;	 And many times have this occurred, and they brought death or harm to others on several occasions.

des brus qui vienent sor la sodure	 Of those who come from the disorder

de la dislocation de l’espaule	 "The dislocation of the shoulder.

li jointure reva ens maintenant.	 The joint will be reset now.
Et quant elle est ens, en quel maniere que ce soit, si covient que tu mettes desoz l’assele une spere de laine igal, puis met l’emplaustre aparilliet de poudre dou molin, avec encens et aubun d’uef, sus toute l’espaule et entor, puis l’estrain desoz l’assele avenanment, et torne le liien sus l’emplaustre, et embraice la main a son col, et soit li mains demorans ensi.	 In case the dislocation occurs on the right shoulder, first apply gentle pressure from below to try and reset it back into place; then gently massage the area with powder of molin (a type of coarse flour), along with incense and saffron, all over the shoulder and arm; repeat this process until the joint is repositioned correctly.
Et covient qu’il menjuce poc, tant que li membres soit confortez, car il sanera plus tost;	 It is advisable to hold it gently as long as the limbs are comfortable because he will heal faster.
et puis menjuce plus aprés V jors ou VII, et le mueve;	 And then move after three or seven days, it moves again;
et s’il est fermeis et il n’est mollifiez, si est sanez.	 If the veins are firm and not relaxed, if there is swelling.

et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie;	 And put on an splint, and fix the limb into place securely, and tie it with strong cords, then release it.
et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.	 Do not force the dislocated joint to move, as long as the limbs are comfortable.
Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez	 "And as for limbs that are unable to move due to severe treatment in healing the ache, until they become whole.
de la dislocation dou talon	 of the shoulder
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	 The arms cannot move at all or fully extend and straighten out completely.
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee:	 And if it is suspected that the bone is displaced, try first at the part where there has been damage.
li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	 Here is the translation: "The man should gently extend his hands when he is sitting alone.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville;	 And when standing upright, if it's convenient that you sit with your right side forward and the elbow touches the knee.
puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut;	 Then press it to one of your hands and then switch to the other hand, repeat this three times, and hold it high for a moment.
et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet;	 And do that two more times as we have said, removing and stretching the shoulder.
s’elle revient, c’est bien;	 If it comes back, you're good to go.
se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient;	 But if not, repeat the process as we have said, for it may come back.
et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide;	 And if it does not come back after that process, sit on the ground with your elbow between your knees and hold the shoulder down firmly until it stops.
puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet;	 Here is the first sentence to translate.
puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent;	 After that, these ministers are gently applied all over, and should be pressed between the two sides of the wound to hold it in place while the wound is being treated.
puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	 Then apply ice packs gently all over and press them between the two sides of the dislocation to hold it in place until it settles down.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois;	 And when it reaches the point of needing staples and stitches, press them in place, form the wound and hold the arm to the leg, while firm but not too tight.
puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain;	 Then let it rest for two or three days, be gentle with the patient if stitches are required.
puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors;	 After that, remove them after one day to four days and treat the wound for another two or three days.
et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	 And if he stands at this end, it is still necessary to straighten him as well.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 "And the patient should avoid doing this, as we've said before, until it is healed.
des dois	 "The second one does not
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	 "When the two are loosened, if it's convenient to stretch gently while working on them.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne;	 And if dislocations occur in no less than two joints, make sure to straighten the affected limb at its point of origin or attachment, and keep your finger on that joint while pressing down firmly until it straightens.
et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie;	 And when the dislocations are gone and no longer cause any pain, if you have identified two joints as the source of the problem, then straighten them out and let go after three tries.
et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And keep it at rest until it is healed completely.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	 Of injury and dislocation combined
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert:	 When there are dislocations along with wounds and injuries that come and go many times,
si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis;	 if you are not skillful in the art and you do not apply it properly for a long time, nor show mercy or compassion to others.
et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit;	 "And begin with gentle care, leave the patient's hand free of pain. Do you not see hope for recovery?
et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne;	 And when you do see hope, gently stretch the limb back to its place.
et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis;	 And when the limbs are in place, administer gentle care as needed to heal wounds.
et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples;	 "And with dislocation and fractures, attend medical attention if necessary, and follow the instructions given in simple injuries.
et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	 "And be cautious of entering into a state of fear, as I have mentioned, for it is not good according to your Creator, and for the safety of you and your body.
